# 2026-05-21 · quant-ph 论文速递


## LEAD：量子坦纳码的局部集合辅助并行解码框架

**Original Title:** LEAD: A Local Ensemble-Assisted Parallel Decoding Framework for Quantum Tanner Codes

**Authors:** Zhuo-Yan Xiao, Sha Shi, Chen-Peng Huang, Dong-Sheng Wang, Yun-Jiang Wang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17796v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.17796v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

量子坦纳码是最近开发的一类量子错误纠正码，其特征是良好的渐进性能特征。尽管具有理论潜力，但有效利用其结构特性的实用解码算法仍然有限。这项工作介绍了LEAD（本地集合辅助解码器），这是一种为量子Tanner码量身定制的结构感知解码框架。所提出的方案利用凯莱复合体的可分解结构将全局码投影到由顶点邻居定义的重叠局部子码上，其中并行估计错误概率。为了确保全局一致性，LEAD利用综合体固有的拓扑对称性，并引入软信息正规化机制来缓解信息聚合期间的局部过度自信。该框架支持高度并行、低复杂性的解码，本质上与各种本地搜索启发式方法兼容。模拟结果表明，LEAD的逻辑错误率比标准解码框架明显低，同时大幅减少了平均解码延迟和迭代次数。


### Abstract

Quantum Tanner codes are a recently developed family of quantum error-correcting codes characterized by favorable asymptotic performance characteristics. Despite their theoretical potential, practical decoding algorithms that effectively leverage their structural properties remain limited. This work introduces LEAD (Local Ensemble-Assisted Decoder), a structure-aware decoding framework tailored for quantum Tanner codes. The proposed scheme leverages the decomposable structure of Cayley complexes to project the global code onto overlapping local subcodes defined by vertex neighborhoods, where error probabilities are estimated in parallel. To ensure global consistency, LEAD utilizes the inherent topological symmetry of the complex and introduces a soft-information regularization mechanism to mitigate local overconfidence during information aggregation. This framework enables highly parallelized, low-complexity decoding that is intrinsically compatible with various local search heuristics. Simulation results demonstrate that LEAD achieves significantly lower logical error rates than standard decoding framework while substantially reducing the average decoding latency and iteration count.


---


## 光子-原子粒度噪声测温

**Original Title:** Photon-Atom Granularity Noise Thermometry

**Authors:** Chen-Rong Liu, Yixuan Wang, Xiaowei Wang, Chuang Li, Mingti Zhou, Runxia Tao, Hongwei Chen, Ying Dong

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17797v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.17797v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们提出了粒度噪音测温法（GNT），这是一种基于波动的光学测温方案，利用原子离散性引起的极化率的内在波动。传输光的功率谱密度表现出高于散粒噪音极限的过量噪音，该噪音与光原子比$\mathCal{R}$呈线性缩放。因此，改变射入功率（因此$\mathCal{R}$）会产生该线性缩放的斜坡$\mathCal{K}$，该线性缩放直接编码温度。通过等离子体分散函数推导出极化率矩的封闭式表达，从而产生不同的温度标度：热蒸汽的$\mathcal{K}\propto P_{\mathcalm {v}}（T）/T^2$，冷原子的$\mathcal{K}\propto T^{2}$。虽然实际实施需要仔细控制技术噪音和系统参数，但本框架为使用原子系组的光学测温提供了基于噪音的路径。


### Abstract

We propose granularity noise thermometry (GNT), a fluctuation-based optical thermometry scheme that exploits the intrinsic fluctuations of susceptibility arising from atomic discreteness. The power spectral density of transmitted light exhibits an excess noise above the shot-noise limit that scales linearly with the photon-to-atom ratio $\mathcal{R}$. Consequently, varying the incident power (hence $\mathcal{R}$) yields the slope $\mathcal{K}$ of this linear scaling, which directly encodes the temperature. Closed-form expressions for the polarizability moments are derived via the plasma dispersion function, which yield distinct temperature scalings: $\mathcal{K}\propto P_{\mathrm{v}}(T)/T^2$ for thermal vapors and $\mathcal{K}\propto T^{2}$ for cold atoms. While practical implementation requires careful control of technical noise and system parameters, the present framework provides a noise-based pathway for optical thermometry using atomic ensembles.


---


## 非平衡SU（1，1）干涉仪产生超短脉冲序列中确定性多模强度压缩

**Original Title:** Generation of deterministic multi-mode intensity squeezing in a train of ultra-short pulses by unbalanced SU(1,1) interferometers

**Authors:** Wen Zhao, Xiao Liu, Yunxiao Zhang, Xueshi Guo, Xiaoying Li

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17798v2

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.17798v2

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

时分多路传输光参数放大器（OPA）产生的连续可变量子态因其扩大模尺度的潜力而具有吸引力。目前，由于OPA是由连续波激光器抽运的，时间模的持续时间超过100 ns，这限制了量子态的规模。在这里，我们通过使用不平衡SU（1，1）干涉仪（USUI）演示了局部化在持续时间为$10 $ ps的短脉冲序列中的多模式强度压缩，其中锁模激光器被用作泵，并通过光延迟和非线性分束器的组合实现了时间域多路传输。使用脉冲分辨联合测量，我们揭示了状态的相关结构是独特的，并且与以前的方法有根本不同。由于全球量子相关性，强度压缩不仅取决于OPA的收益，还与联合测量的模数$M$有关。我们通过实验在30种模式之间进行了联合测量，并表明当$M>10$时，强度噪音比散粒噪音水平低$\sim0.9 $分贝。我们的研究为通过脉冲泵运USUI产生超大规模量子态打开了大门。


### Abstract

The continuous variable quantum state generated by time-domain multiplexed optical parametric amplifier (OPA) is attractive because of the potential of enlarging the mode scale. Currently, the duration of temporal mode is longer than 100 ns since the OPA is pumped by the continuous wave laser, which restricts the scale of quantum state. Here we demonstrate multi-mode intensity squeezing localized in a train of short pulses with duration of $\sim10$ ps by using an unbalanced SU(1,1) interferometer (USUI), where the mode-locked laser is exploited as the pump and the time-domain multiplexing is realized by the combination of optical delay and nonlinear beam splitter. Using the pulse resolved joint measurements, we reveal the correlation structure of the state is unique and fundamentally different from previous approaches. Due to the globe quantum correlation, the intensity squeezing not only depends on the gain of OPAs but also ties to the mode number $M$ of joint measurement. We experimentally perform joint measurement among 30 modes and show the intensity noise lower than shot noise level by $\sim0.9$ dB is achievable for $M>10$. Our investigations open the door for generating ultra-large scale quantum state by pulse pumped USUI.


---


## 多体自由电子W态纠缠的产生

**Original Title:** Heralded Generation of Multipartite Free-Electron W-State Entanglement

**Authors:** Du Ran, Jing-Yi Liu, Dan Jin, Shuai Liu, Reuven Ianconescu, Ze-Long He, Ji-Yuan Bai, Ya-dong Li, Avraham Gover

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17802v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.17802v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们提出了一种预示性的协议，用于在边带分解的相互作用机制中从原子$W_N$资源产生多方自由电子纠缠。该方案由N$独立的电子-原子相互作用臂组成，其中每个自由电子局部耦合到一个两级系统。对于均匀耦合和常见的失调，动力学在脉冲逼近下进行解析求解。将原子投影到全接地状态将初始原子激发流映射到电子上边带流，并准备精确的$N$-电子$W_N$-型状态。以封闭形式获得共振和失调区域的预示概率。在共振时，最佳成功概率服从大的-$N$缩放$P_{G_N}' x}\sim e '/N$。预示状态保留了原子资源的多方纠缠结构，如任意$N$所示，并明确说明$N=3$。讨论了失调、弱对称性破缺、超旋转波修正和高斯耦合包封。该协议提供了一条可扩展的途径，从量子电子光学内的局部原子资源产生多方自由电子纠缠。


### Abstract

We propose a heralded protocol for generating multipartite free-electron entanglement from atomic $W_N$ resources in a sideband-resolved interaction regime. The scheme consists of $N$ independent electron--atom interaction arms, where each free electron couples locally to one two-level system. For uniform couplings and common detuning, the dynamics is solved analytically within the rotating-wave approximation. Projecting the atoms onto the all-ground state maps the initial atomic excitation manifold onto the electronic upper-sideband manifold and prepares an exact $N$-electron $W_N$-type state. The heralding probability is obtained in closed form for resonant and detuned regimes. At resonance, the optimal success probability obeys the large-$N$ scaling $P_{G_N}^{\max}\sim e^{-1}/N$. The heralded state retains the multipartite entanglement structure of the atomic resource, as shown for arbitrary $N$ and illustrated explicitly for $N=3$. Detuning, weak symmetry breaking, beyond-rotating-wave corrections, and Gaussian coupling envelopes are discussed. The protocol provides a scalable route toward multipartite free-electron entanglement generation from localized atomic resources within quantum electron optics.


---


## 可扩展离子俘获量子处理器的低温时分多路传输电压控制

**Original Title:** Cryogenic Time-Division-Multiplexed Voltage Control for Scalable Trapped-Ion Quantum Processors

**Authors:** Ryutaro Ohira, Shinichi Morisaka, Yoshinori Kurimoto, Toshiaki Inada, Ippei Nakamura, Takefumi Miyoshi, Atsushi Noguchi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17824v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.17824v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

基于量子电荷耦合器件架构的俘获离子量子计算机每个量子位需要大约十个陷阱电极，这使得真空反馈器的数量成为系统规模的瓶颈。针对陷阱电极的基于时分多路传输（时分多路传输）的电压控制提供了缓解这种限制的自然途径。然而，之前的研究仅限于静态陷阱势补偿和动态电极控制的室温演示的架构提案，而静态和动态电极的基于IDM的电压控制的低温操作尚未进行实验探索。在这项研究中，我们针对两种不同的电极类别开发并低温验证了基于时分多址的电压控制方案。对于用于陷阱电压补偿的静态电极，我们实施了一个在约27 K下工作的32通道解多路分解系统，实现了37.5 GHz的有效电压更新率，输出范围为$\pm10 ~\mathrm{V}$每个通道。对于离子操作（例如穿梭）中使用的动态电极，我们实施了一个在大约14~K下工作的四通道解多路分解系统，实现了1~MHz的有效电压更新率和相当的输出范围。这些结果确立了基于时分多址的电压控制作为两种电极类别的实用方法，为缓解可扩展的离子俘获量子处理器中的真空穿通瓶颈提供了途径。


### Abstract

Trapped-ion quantum computers based on the quantum charge-coupled device architecture require on the order of ten trap electrodes per qubit, making the number of vacuum feedthroughs a bottleneck at the system scale. Time-division multiplexed (TDM)-based voltage control for trap electrodes provides a natural route to alleviate this constraint. However, previous studies have been limited to architectural proposals for static trap-potential compensation and room-temperature demonstrations of dynamic-electrode control, leaving cryogenic operation of TDM-based voltage control for static and dynamic electrodes experimentally unexplored. In this study, we develop and cryogenically validate TDM-based voltage control schemes for two distinct electrode classes. For static electrodes used in trap-potential compensation, we implement a 32-channel demultiplexed system operating at approximately 27~K, achieving an effective voltage update rate of 37.5~kHz with an output range of $\pm10~\mathrm{V}$ per channel. For dynamic electrodes used in ion operations, such as shuttling, we implement a four-channel demultiplexed system operating at approximately 14~K, achieving an effective voltage update rate of 1~MHz with a comparable output range. These results establish TDM-based voltage control as a practical approach for both electrode classes, providing a path for mitigating the vacuum feedthrough bottleneck in scalable trapped-ion quantum processors.


---


## 远离平衡的超流氦集体激发的相关光谱

**Original Title:** Coherent spectroscopy of collective excitations in superfluid helium far from equilibrium

**Authors:** Gabriel Voith, Alexander A. Milner, Valery Milner

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17835v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.17835v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

超流体中集体激发的超快动力学在roton状态之外基本上尚未被探索，尽管它对于理解这些系统中的非平衡过程很重要。在这里，我们采用超快相干控制和超短脉冲序列，对远离平衡的超流氦中兰道激发光谱的多个分支进行光谱分析。通过测量时间分辨光学双折射，我们追踪了Maxon对和Pitaevskii平台激发的非平衡动力学以及之前研究的roton对，揭示了Maxon对令人惊讶的强大结合能、其极短的寿命以及准粒子有效质量对相关响应的影响。这些结果证明了通过探测其在费米和微微秒时间尺度上的非平衡动力学来提取之前无法获得的有关强相互作用量子流体中集体激发的信息的能力。


### Abstract

Ultrafast dynamics of collective excitations in superfluids remains largely unexplored beyond the roton regime, despite its importance for understanding nonequilibrium processes in these systems. Here, we employ ultrafast coherent control with sequences of femtosecond pulses to perform spectroscopy of multiple branches of the Landau excitation spectrum in superfluid helium far from equilibrium. By measuring the time-resolved optical birefringence, we track the nonequilibrium dynamics of maxon pairs and Pitaevskii plateau excitations alongside the previously studied roton pairs, revealing surprisingly strong binding energy of maxon pairs, their extremely short lifetime, and the influence of the quasiparticle effective mass on the phase of the coherent response. These results demonstrate the ability to extract previously inaccessible information about collective excitations in a strongly interacting quantum fluid by probing its nonequilibrium dynamics on femtosecond and picosecond timescales.


---


## 巨原子光管设置中通过相调制研究连续体中的束缚态和动力学

**Original Title:** Bound state in the continuum and dynamics via phase modulation in giant-atom waveguide setups

**Authors:** Ji Qi, Xiaojun Zhang, Honngwei Yu, Zhihai Wang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17878v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.17878v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

巨原子通过超出偶极逼近的多个空间分离的连接点耦合到一个导体，为基于连续体中干扰诱导束缚状态（CIC）的量子信息处理提供了一种通用途径。虽然多巨原子架构正在朝着巨原子量子网络发展，但巨原子之间的直接耦合，特别是相关的耦合相，在原子动力学中的作用仍然没有得到充分的理解。在这里，我们通过研究两个巨原子波导QED模型，迈出了解决这个问题的第一步。我们表明，耦合相可以用于控制CIC的数量及其对量子和原子的分布。更有趣的是，CIC的存在引起了各种动力学行为，为调整巨原子波导QED系统中的量子状态演变提供了有效的机制。我们的结果强调了耦合相工程作为控制非局部光-物质界面中干涉、束缚态和量子动力学的有用工具。


### Abstract

Giant atoms, which couple to a waveguide through multiple spatially separated connection points beyond the dipole approximation, provide a versatile route for quantum information processing based on interference-induced bound states in the continuum (BICs). While multi-giant-atom architectures are being developed toward giant-atom quantum networks, the role of direct coupling between the giant atoms, in particular the associated coupling phase, in atomic dynamics remains insufficiently understood. Here we take a first step toward addressing this issue by studying a two-giant-atom waveguide-QED model. We show that the coupling phase can be used to control both the number of BICs and their profiles for both of photon and atoms. More interestingly, the presence of BICs gives rise to a variety of dynamical behaviors, providing an effective mechanism for tailoring quantum-state evolution in giant-atom waveguide-QED systems. Our results highlight coupling-phase engineering as a useful tool for controlling interference, bound states, and quantum dynamics in nonlocal light--matter interfaces.


---


## 具有矩阵积状态的量子Hilbert空间中的几何原型学习

**Original Title:** Geometric Prototype Learning in Quantum Hilbert Space with Matrix Product States

**Authors:** Kun Zhang, Lei Ding, Sheng-Chen Bai, Jing Sun, An-Qi Jing, Min Tang, Shi-Ju Ran

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17895v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.17895v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

量子概率提供了一种新颖的框架，用于在希尔伯特空间中制定机器学习（ML）问题。我们引入了一种基于原型的学习方案，其中类代表被编码为生成矩阵产品状态（MPS）。由于这些原型与量子编码数据样本位于同一个希尔伯特空间中，因此可以通过量子状态的几何测量来执行分类和集群等各种ML任务。这种方法将原型学习从经典特征空间提升到量子希尔伯特空间。Fashion-MNIST和真实心电图数据集上的基准测试表明，我们的方法优于经典的原型方法，同时与标准的黑盒神经网络保持竞争力。我们还确定了一个“吸引力”的量子概率原型引起的效果，并介绍了基于原型距离的降维方案。我们的研究结果建立了量子态作为原型学习的可解释框架，为在量子希尔伯特空间中设计ML算法开辟了新的方向。


### Abstract

Quantum probability provides a novel framework for formulating machine-learning (ML) problems in Hilbert space. We introduce a prototype-based learning scheme where class representatives are encoded as generative matrix product states (MPS). Because these prototypes reside in the same Hilbert space as quantum-encoded data samples, various ML tasks such as classification and clustering can be performed through geometric measures of quantum states. This approach lifts prototype learning from classical feature space to quantum Hilbert space. Benchmarks on Fashion-MNIST and a real-world electrocardiogram dataset demonstrate that our method outperforms classical prototype approaches while remaining competitive with standard black-box neural networks. We also identify an ``attraction'' effect induced by the quantum-probabilistic prototypes and introduce a dimensionality-reduction scheme based on prototype distances. Our results establish quantum states as an explainable framework for prototype learning, opening new directions for designing ML algorithms in quantum Hilbert space.


---


## 开放系统中操作员的量子Mpemba效应

**Original Title:** Quantum Mpemba effect for operators in open systems

**Authors:** Pitambar Bagui, Bijay Kumar Agarwalla

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17908v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.17908v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

量子Mpemba效应涉及在正正动力学或非正动力学下演变的量子状态的异常松弛。在开放量子系统的背景下，虽然大多数研究都集中在Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad（GKSL）主方程所描述的完全正的踪迹动力学下演变的量子状态，但我们证明了类似的效应可以在操作员的水平上产生。特别是，我们表明，在伴随Liouvillian下进化的操作符--尽管不是痕迹保留地图--仍然可以表现出真正的Mpemba效应。我们推导出这种现象发生的一般条件，并验证了我们对三种不同开放量子设置的预测。我们的结果拓宽了量子系统中Mpemba效应的范围，并提供了一个框架，用于控制物理相关的可观测量的弛豫。


### Abstract

The quantum Mpemba effect concerns with anomalous relaxation of quantum states that evolves either under unitary or non-unitary dynamics. In the context of open quantum systems, while most studies focus on quantum states evolving under completely positive trace-presing dynamics described by the Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad (GKSL) master equation, we demonstrate that an analogous effect can arise at the level of operators. In particular, we show that operators that evolves under the adjoint Liouvillian -- despite not being a trace-preserving map -- can still exhibit a genuine Mpemba effect. We derive general conditions under which this phenomenon can occur and validate our predictions for three different open quantum setups. Our results broaden the scope of the Mpemba effect in quantum systems and provide a framework for controlling the relaxation of physically relevant observables.


---


## 异相量子气体混合物中的温控共振

**Original Title:** Temperature-Controlled Resonance in a Heteronuclear Quantum Gas Mixture

**Authors:** Xiaoyi Yang, Tianyu Xu, Shengli Ma, Zhigang Wu, Ren Zhang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17931v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.17931v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

单通道共振是原子散射的基本过程，但它们的发生在很大程度上是偶然的，缺乏系统控制。在这封信中，我们提出了一种通过控制异相混合物的温度来实现连续可调单通道共振的机制。通过将类卡西米尔介导的相互作用扩展到有限温度，我们证明费米表面的热涂抹重塑了杂质之间的有效势，从而在很宽的参数范围内产生温控共振（TLR）。其直接结果是，共振位置随着温度变化而系统性地移动，从而为该机制提供了清晰的实验特征。我们进一步研究了沉浸在费米海中的玻色气体的激冷动力学，并证明最近实验中观察到的温度相关损失特征与TLR机制一致。我们的结果将温度确立为超冷量子气体单通道共振的简单且实验可访问的控制旋钮。


### Abstract

Single-channel resonances are fundamental processes in scattering of atoms, yet their occurrence is largely incidental and lacks systematic control. In this Letter, we propose a mechanism to realize a continuously tunable single-channel resonance by controlling the temperature of the heteronuclear mixture. By extending the Casimir-like mediated interaction to finite temperature, we demonstrate that thermal smearing of the Fermi surface reshapes the effective potential between impurities, giving rise to a temperature-controlled resonance (TCR) over a wide parameter range. As a direct consequence, the resonance position shifts systematically with temperature variation, providing a clear experimental signature of this mechanism. We further investigate the quench dynamics of a Bose gas immersed in a Fermi sea and demonstrate that the observed temperature-dependent loss features in recent experiments are consistent with the TCR mechanism. Our results establish temperature as a simple and experimentally accessible control knob for single-channel resonances in ultracold quantum gases.


---


## 时间问题：路径积分观

**Original Title:** The problem of time: a path integral view

**Authors:** Juan Manuel Diaz, Alejandro Perez

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17935v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.17935v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们表明，时间演化在一个永恒的非相对论封闭量子系统中的出现--被视为一般协变量子理论的穷人模型--可以从路径积分表示的角度来理解。正如函数积分方法中经常发生的那样，这种观点为在操作员/Hilbert空间公式中变得繁琐的特征提供了更直观的描述。我们展示了一旦时钟自由度被确定并置于合适的半经典“好时钟状态”，薛定格进化是如何出现的。   我们的分析的结果扩展到具有作用$S$（包括重力）的一般协变系统的路径积分公式。在此类理论中，某些转变幅度采取$\BEP（iS/\hbar）+\BEP（-iS/\hbar）$的形式，而不是预期的“前向传播”$\BEP（iS/\hbar）$。这个特征被称为{\em cos问题}，出现在路径积分的具体规则化中，例如在定义环量子引力中旋转网络状态之间的物理内能积的旋转泡沫表示中。无论是在形式上还是在显式正规化中，这种明显的困难都导致一些作者寻求修改基本幅度以消除反向传播。   我们的模型表明，cos问题是基本动力学的时间逆转不变性以及过渡幅度中常用的时间中性边界状态的自然结果。当识别合适的时钟系统并将其置于半经典的“良好时钟状态”时，它会引入一个时间箭头，选择“前向传播”$\BEP（iS/\hbar）$，而不会修改基本动态。   该分析澄清了时间如何在合适的条件下出现，并强调在规范公式中，量子引力从根本上是永恒的。


### Abstract

We show that the emergence of time evolution in an otherwise timeless nonrelativistic closed quantum system -- viewed as a poor man's model of generally covariant quantum theory -- can be understood from the perspective of the path integral representation. As often happens in the functional integral approach, this viewpoint offers a more intuitive account of features that become cumbersome in the operator/Hilbert-space formulation. We show how Schrödinger evolution emerges once a clock degree of freedom is identified and placed in a suitable semiclassical `good-clock state'.
  Our analysis has a consequence that extends to path integral formulations of generally covariant systems with action $S$ (including gravity). In such theories certain transition amplitudes take the form $\exp(iS/\hbar)+\exp(-iS/\hbar)$ rather than the expected `forward propagating' $\exp(iS/\hbar)$. This feature, known as the {\em cosine problem}, appears in concrete regularizations of the path integral, for example in the spin foam representation defining the physical inner product between spin network states in loop quantum gravity. Both formally and in explicit regularizations, this apparent difficulty has led some authors to seek modifications of the basic amplitudes to eliminate backward propagation.
  Our model shows that the cosine problem is instead a natural consequence of time-reversal invariance of the fundamental dynamics together with the time-neutral boundary states commonly used in transition amplitudes. When a suitable clock system is identified and placed in a semiclassical `good-clock state', it introduces a time arrow selecting the `forward propagating' $\exp(iS/\hbar)$, without modifying the fundamental dynamics.
  The analysis clarifies how time emerges under suitable conditions and emphasizes that, in the canonical formulation, quantum gravity is fundamentally timeless.


---


## 量子计算环境中分布式工作流的系统感知资源分配

**Original Title:** A System Aware Resource Allocation for Distributed Workflows in Quantum Computing Environments

**Authors:** Abhishek Sawaika, Udaya Parampalli, Rajkumar Buyya

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17944v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.17944v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

提供量子计算功能访问的基于云的平台的快速发展为这些高度敏感且昂贵的设备的有效使用带来了几个挑战。尽管当前的大多数系统使用基于优先级的访问协议，但它们无法完全支持大规模应用程序的可靠、高效和可扩展的执行。为了克服这一限制，我们提出了一种全面的解决方案，用于将量子程序有效分配到适当的量子设备，同时考虑到所有相关的成本指标，包括保真度、执行时间和通信费用。我们还制定了分布式量子工作流程的用例，并提出了修改后的基于图的算法来解决此类用例的分配问题，假设是混合的经典量子网络。由于大型独立设备的硬件进步是一个持续的过程，因此研究此类分布式工作流程以最大限度地利用当前NISQ设备至关重要。我们的实证研究表明，对于几乎所有评估参数，所提出的技术都比最先进的方法表现得更好，执行时间平均改善约5美元，通信费用平均改善约30美元，等待时间平均改善40美元，保真度改善2美元，为高效分配策略提供了更好的解决方案。


### Abstract

Rapid advancements in cloud based platforms providing access to quantum computing capabilities have opened up several challenges for efficient usage of these highly delicate and costly devices. Although most of the current systems use a priority based access protocol, they are unable to fully support reliable, efficient, and scalable execution of larger-scale applications. To overcome this limitation, we propose a comprehensive solution for efficient allocation of quantum programs to appropriate quantum devices, considering all the relevant cost metrics into account including, fidelity, execution time and communication overhead. We also formulate use-cases for distributed quantum workflow and propose modified graph based algorithms to solve for allocation of such use-cases, assuming a hybrid classical-quantum network. Since hardware advancements in large standalone devices is an ongoing process, it is critical to investigate such distributed workflows to maximize the best utilization of current NISQ devices. Our empirical study shows that the proposed techniques perform better than state-of-the-art methods for almost all evaluation parameters, with average improvements of approximately $5\%$ in execution time, $30\%$ in communication overhead, $40\%$ in wait time and $2\%$ in fidelity, providing better solutions to efficient allocation strategies.

## 3D分数格族中的安德森转变和迁移边缘

**Original Title:** Anderson Transition and Mobility Edges in a Family of 3D Fractal Lattices

**Authors:** Tianyu Li, Xin Tang, Sheng Liu, Haiping Hu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17953v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.17953v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

安德森局部化从根本上受维度控制，但连续可调非整维度中安德森转变的本质在很大程度上仍然没有被探索。在这里，我们引入了一系列具有连续可调谱维度$d_s\in[2，3]$的三维分数格，为研究超越整维和跨较低临界维度的局部物理提供了一个受控平台$d_s=2$。使用大规模有限尺寸缩放分析，我们系统地研究安德森转变并识别整个分数家族的移动性边缘。随着光谱维度从2美元增加到3美元，严重障碍强度从0美元持续演变到16.6美元。我们表明，谱维度主要决定了转变的普适性类别，而精确的临界点还受到底层分数格的微观几何细节的影响。临界指数表现出对$d_s$的大致反向依赖，为非整维中的标度理论提供了定量见解。我们的结果建立了可调的分数格作为探索传统整维系统之外的局部化和量子临界现象的通用框架。


### Abstract

Anderson localization is fundamentally controlled by dimensionality, yet the nature of the Anderson transition in continuously tunable noninteger dimensions remains largely unexplored. Here, we introduce a family of three-dimensional fractal lattices with continuously tunable spectral dimension $d_s\in[2,3]$, providing a controlled platform for studying localization physics beyond integer dimensions and across the lower critical dimension $d_s=2$. Using large-scale finite-size scaling analysis, we systematically investigate the Anderson transition and identify mobility edges throughout the fractal family. The critical disorder strength evolves continuously from $0$ to $16.6$ as the spectral dimension increases from $2$ to $3$. We show that the spectral dimension predominantly governs the universality class of the transition, while the precise critical point is additionally influenced by microscopic geometric details of the underlying fractal lattice. The critical exponent exhibits an approximate inverse dependence on $d_s$, providing quantitative insight into scaling theory in noninteger dimensions. Our results establish tunable fractal lattices as a versatile framework for exploring localization and quantum critical phenomena beyond conventional integer-dimensional systems.


---


## 测量纠缠双量子场的完整空间施密特模式

**Original Title:** Measuring the complete set of spatial Schmidt modes of entangled two-photon fields

**Authors:** Radhika Prasad, Nilakshi Senapati, Abhinandan Bhattacharjee, Suman Karan, Anand K. Jha

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17974v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.17974v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

自发参数下转换（SPDC）是最广泛使用的多维纠缠双量子态来源，空间自由度中的纠缠被认为最适合利用多维优势。尽管施密特基为任何自由度的纠缠双量子态的状态描述提供了自然选择，但目前还没有技术可以测量纠缠双量子场的施密特基。现有技术只能在先验已知施密特基时重建施密特谱。相比之下，我们提出了一种在没有任何先验知识的情况下测量完整的空间施密特模式的技术。使用这种技术，我们报告了具有超过3000个施密特模式（迄今为止报道的最高值）的状态测量，其保真度高达98$\%$。我们希望我们的工作能够显着推进基于SPDC的系统中多维优势的利用。


### Abstract

Spontaneous parametric down-conversion (SPDC) is the most widely-used source of high-dimensional entangled two-photon states, and the entanglement in the spatial degree of freedom is considered best suited for harnessing high-dimensional advantages. Although the Schmidt basis provides a natural choice for state characterisation of entangled two-photon states in any degree of freedom, there is currently no technique that can measure the Schmidt basis of an entangled two-photon field. The existing techniques can only reconstruct the Schmidt spectrum when the Schmidt basis is known a priori. In contrast, we present a technique that measures the complete set of spatial Schmidt modes without any prior knowledge. Using this technique, we report measurement of states with over 3000 Schmidt modes -- highest reported yet -- with up to 98$\%$ fidelity. We expect our work to significantly advance the harnessing of high-dimensional advantages in SPDC-based systems.

## 通过非阿贝尔量子几何测量探索张量奇异性及其欧拉级后代

**Original Title:** Probing Tensor Singularities and Their Euler-Class Descendants via Non-Abelian Quantum Geometry Measurement

**Authors:** Zhe Wang, Yan-Qing Zhu, Xinsheng Tan, Giandomenico Palumbo, Lichang Ji, Wei Xin, Shi-Liang Zhu, Yang Yu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17977v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.17977v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们报告了对一类新的二维（4D）张量奇异性及其三维（3D）欧拉级后代的理论预测和实验观察，这些子子孙受到了超导电路平台上的手征和时空倒置对称性的保护。观察到4D点状奇异性/毛刺，其特征在于与张量规范场相关的实束gerbe的Dixmier-Douady类，在保毛刺的扰动下演变成携带额外的第一欧拉类电荷的节环。降维揭示了3D欧拉和欧拉弯曲偶极，表现出非平凡的欧拉布局和一个能够确保零能量平坦带即使没有相互作用也继承非平凡的布局的拓和规则。至关重要的是，这些多维简并系统是使用混合模拟-数字协议来映射和重建的，该协议专为超量子位阵列内的非阿贝尔量子几何测量而设计的。我们的工作不仅扩展了拓扑单子家族，而且还建立了一个强大的实验框架，用于探索跨不同量子平台的高级规范理论和实束布局。


### Abstract

We report the theoretical prediction and experimental observation of a new class of four-dimensional (4D) tensor singularities and their three-dimensional (3D) Euler-class descendants, protected by chiral and spacetime inversion symmetries on a superconducting circuit platform. The 4D point-like singularity/monopole, characterized by the Dixmier-Douady class of a real bundle gerbe associated with tensor gauge fields, is observed to evolve into a nodal ring carrying an additional first Euler class charge under symmetry-preserving perturbations. Dimensional reduction reveals 3D Euler and Euler curvature dipoles, exhibiting nontrivial Euler topology and a topological sum rule that ensures zero-energy flat bands inherit nontrivial topology even without interactions. Crucially, these high-dimensional degenerate systems are mapped and reconstructed using a hybrid analog-digital protocol designed for non-Abelian quantum geometry measurement within a superconducting qubit array. Our work not only expands the family of topological monopoles but also establishes a robust experimental framework for exploring high-order gauge theory and real-bundle topology across diverse quantum platforms.

## 麦克拉克兰预测的病态薛定格后向扩散的简化动力学

**Original Title:** McLachlan-projected reduced dynamics for ill-posed Schrödingerized backward diffusion

**Authors:** Jeongbin Jo

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17996v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.17996v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

向后扩散是一种原型病态进化：高空间频率随时间呈指数级增长，因此在没有显式正规化的情况下基于网格的时间推进很快就会被噪音淹没。薛定格化将半离散生成器嵌入扩展空间上的埃尔米特动力学中;我们询问麦克拉克兰投影到固定低维框架上是否提供了一个结构化的正规化器，其误差预算可以从投影缺陷中读取，投影缺陷将完全提升传播与简化轨迹分开。我们证明了约化流的唯一性、格拉姆模保守性、根据该缺陷的提升-约化间隙界，以及在统计估计矩阵元素时突出矩阵条件化的扰动估计。我们还阐明了一个相当经典的基线--在同一半离散模型上进行频谱低通或Tikhonov过滤，带宽或山脊强度与所选帧的信息内容相匹配--因此数字对比隔离了薛定格化的简化管道，而不是非正规化的Crank--尼科尔森进行曲，主要展示爆炸。经过校准的一维基准将光谱截断的参考与快照构建的子空间进化和有限镜头QisKit Aer估计配对，说明了提升层、投影层和采样层如何对总体误差产生不同的影响。


### Abstract

Backward diffusion is a prototype ill-posed evolution: high spatial frequencies grow exponentially in time, so mesh-based time marching without explicit regularization is quickly overwhelmed by noise. Schrödingerization embeds the semidiscrete generator into Hermitian dynamics on an extended space; we ask whether McLachlan projection onto a fixed low-dimensional frame supplies a structured regularizer whose error budget can be read from a projection defect that separates full lifted propagation from the reduced trajectory. We prove uniqueness of the reduced flow, Gram-norm conservation, a lifted--reduced gap bound in terms of that defect, and perturbation estimates that highlight overlap-matrix conditioning when matrix elements are estimated statistically. We also spell out a fair classical baseline -- spectral low-pass or Tikhonov filtering on the same semidiscrete model, with bandwidth or ridge strength matched to the information content of the chosen frame -- so numerical contrasts isolate the Schrödingerized reduced pipeline rather than an unregularized Crank--Nicolson march that mainly showcases blow-up. A calibrated one-dimensional benchmark pairs a spectrally truncated reference with snapshot-built subspace evolution and finite-shot Qiskit Aer estimation, illustrating how lift, projection, and sampling layers contribute differently to the overall error.

## 用于混合人工智能训练和推理的量子Sidecar架构：状态保护寄存器、无状态重置和重新准备电路和量子权状态展望

**Original Title:** Quantum Sidecar Architectures for Hybrid AI Training and Inference: Stateful Protected Registers, Stateless Reset-and-Reprepare Circuits and Quantum Weight-State Outlook

**Authors:** Y. Mo, G. D. Su

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18031v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18031v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们提出了一个量子Sidecar架构家族，用于未来的混合AI训练和推理。其中心思想不是将整个Transformer存储在一个小的量子存储器中，也不是声称一次性崩溃为一个经过充分训练的模型或最佳答案。相反，我们为连接到经典大型管道的量子协处理器确定了两种物理上不同的操作模式。第一种是有状态保护寄存器模式，其中保护寄存器存储可重复使用的量子资源，而辅助寄存器或临时寄存器执行QND风格的读出。第二种是无状态重置和重新准备模式，其中每个查询准备任务条件量子电路，在有界训练或推理控制变量上进化，测量候选信号，重置量子位并重复。我们使用2/4/6/8受保护量子位密度矩阵QND风格的宇称读出以及一个辅助和QisKit交叉检查来模拟有状态模式。对于无状态模式，我们在结构化候选景观上包括抽象候选更新采样器和电路级QAOA风格的状态载体采样器，然后进行重置开销敏感性分析。由此产生的框架将量子边车定位为有界信号发生器，用于优化器端采样、适配器或专家选择、检索、路由和推理路径建议。作为一种推测性的观点，我们引入了量子权重状态边车：模型控制变量上的限制量子表示，而不是完整经典权重张量的直接编码。


### Abstract

We propose a quantum sidecar architecture family for future hybrid AI training and inference. The central idea is not to store an entire Transformer in a small quantum memory, nor to claim one-shot collapse into a fully trained model or an optimal answer. Instead, we identify two physically distinct operating modes for quantum co-processors attached to classical large-model pipelines. The first is a stateful protected-register mode, in which a protected register stores a reusable quantum resource while an ancilla or temporary register performs QND-style readout. The second is a stateless reset-and-reprepare mode, in which each query prepares a task-conditioned quantum circuit, evolves over bounded training or inference control variables, measures candidate signals, resets the qubits, and repeats. We simulate the stateful mode using 2/4/6/8 protected-qubit density-matrix QND-style parity readout with one ancilla and a Qiskit cross-check. For the stateless mode, we include both an abstract candidate-update sampler and a circuit-level QAOA-style statevector sampler over structured candidate landscapes, followed by reset-overhead sensitivity analysis. The resulting framework positions quantum sidecars as bounded signal generators for optimizer-side sampling, adapter or expert selection, retrieval, routing, and reasoning-path proposal. As a speculative outlook, we introduce quantum weight-state sidecars: restricted quantum representations over model-control variables, not direct encodings of complete classical weight tensors.


---


## 结构$f$-分歧：参数化量子电路中成本函数矩和梯度的紧普适界

**Original Title:** Structural $f$-divergence: Tight universal bounds for cost function moments and gradients in parameterized quantum circuits

**Authors:** Tomohiro Nishiyama, Yoshihiko Hasegawa

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18051v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18051v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

贫瘠的高原现象，其中变分量子算法的成本函数梯度呈指数消失，仍然是近期量子计算的核心障碍。现有的分析通常依赖于t-设计或Haar-随机假设和酉分布水平上的约束量，为参数化量子电路的参数空间上的概率测度设计提供了有限的见解。在本文中，我们介绍了结构的$f$-发散，一个对称的$f$-发散为基础的措施之间的概率分布的参数空间。我们建立分析权衡不等式，约束的差异，在预期的梯度幅度和成本函数的时刻之间的分布PQC和参考分布;平等是通过一个最小的一个量子位，一层ananimals。作为应用，我们推导出避免BP和成本集中的概率测量的必要条件，以及抑制噪音引起的偏差的充分条件。


### Abstract

The barren plateau phenomenon, in which cost-function gradients of variational quantum algorithms vanish exponentially, remains a central obstacle for near-term quantum computing. Existing analyses typically depend on t-design or Haar-random assumptions and bound quantities at the level of unitary distributions, offering limited insight for designing probability measures on the parameter space of parameterized quantum circuits. In this paper, we introduce the structural $f$-divergence, a symmetric $f$-divergence-based measure between probability distributions on the parameter space. We establish analytically trade-off inequalities that bound the discrepancies in the expected gradient magnitude and in the cost-function moments between a distribution on PQC and a reference distribution; equality is attained by a minimal one-qubit, one-layer ansatz. As applications, we derive necessary conditions on probability measures for avoiding BPs and cost concentration, and sufficient conditions that suppress noise-induced deviations.


---


## 四重破坏性创新推荐系统的参数化4-量子位EWL-Dirac-Solow-Swan Hamilton积分的量子博弈电路

**Original Title:** Parameterized 4-Qubit EWL Quantum Game Circuits with Dirac-Solow-Swan Hamiltonian Integration for Quadruple Helix Disruptive Innovation Recommender Systems

**Authors:** Agung Trisetyarso, Fithra Faisal Hastiadi, Kridanto Surendro

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18080v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18080v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们为四螺旋创新生态系统（学术界、工业界、政府和公民社会）中的推荐系统提出了一种新颖的参数化4量子比特分配器-Wilkens-Lewenstein（EWL 1）量子游戏电路。每个螺旋参与者的本地策略操作符$U_{i} = R_y（θ_{i}）$直接通过从欧盟委员会CORDIS Horizon Europe数据库（项目COVend，ID 101045956）中的真实参与者资助数据（\texit{ecContributionary}）中提取的标准化优势权重进行调整。该电路采用多量子位EBL纠缠器，随后进行参数化局部旋转、逆纠缠器和全测量，仅实现22个门和电路深度11，同时扩展为$O（n）$$n$-轮螺旋通信。量子游戏后的测量概率可以作为破坏性创新趋势与持续创新趋势的推荐分数。这些分数随后被映射到狄拉克-索洛-斯旺汉密尔顿量的对角线狄拉克势，从而能够对颠覆性创新下的资本积累和分歧动力学进行时间演变模拟。真实CORDIS四螺旋协作网络的数值实验证明了该电路的NISQ兼容性及其高保真预测破坏性资本轨迹的能力。   提出的框架架起了量子博弈论、参数化量子电路和相对论经济增长模型的桥梁，为复杂社会经济生态系统中的创新政策和战略决策提供了计算高效的工具。通过开放QisKit实现提供复杂性分析和再现性。


### Abstract

We present a novel parameterized 4-qubit Eisert-Wilkens-Lewenstein (EWL) quantum game circuit for recommender systems in quadruple helix innovation ecosystems (academia, industry, government, and civil society). The local strategy operators $U_{i} = R_y(θ_{i})$ for each helix actor are directly tuned by normalized dominance weights extracted from real participant funding data (\texit{ecContribution}) in the European Commission CORDIS Horizon Europe database (project COVend, ID 101045956). The circuit employs a multi-qubit EWL entangler followed by parameterized local rotations, inverse entangler, and full measurement, achieving only 22 gates and circuit depth 11 while scaling as $O(n)$ for $n$-round helix communications. Measurement probabilities after the quantum game serve as recommender scores for disruptive versus sustaining innovation trends. These scores are subsequently mapped into the diagonal Dirac potential of a Dirac-Solow-Swan Hamiltonian, enabling time-evolution simulation of capital accumulation and bifurcation dynamics under disruptive innovation. Numerical experiments on real CORDIS quadruple-helix collaboration networks demonstrate the circuit's NISQ compatibility and its ability to forecast disruptive capital trajectories with high fidelity.
  The proposed framework bridges quantum game theory, parameterized quantum circuits, and relativistic economic growth models, offering a computationally efficient tool for innovation policy and strategic decision-making in complex socio-economic ecosystems. Complexity analysis and reproducibility are provided through open Qiskit implementations.


---


## Fock态传输中的量子特征和半经典限制

**Original Title:** Quantum signatures and semiclassical limitations in the transmission of Fock states

**Authors:** Daniel Julian Nader

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18091v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18091v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

通过势垒的传输是量子力学中的一个基本问题。虽然半经典方法可以逼近传输的某些方面，但它们无法捕捉与维格纳函数负性相关的本质量子干涉。我们数值研究了位移Fock态通过反振子垒的传输，无论有没有克尔非线性，这为实验实现提供了一条潜在的途径。这些状态只能进行大约的经典描述，因为它们特征的维格纳函数负性在相空间中不存在。半经典模拟重现了整体传输，但偏离了确切的结果，并且未能捕捉到维格纳函数负性区域越过屏障时出现的短期平稳期。对于克尔非线性，非线性边界的反射将干涉驱动到经典禁区，这是半经典方法无法达到的效果。我们发现，这些干扰效应不会改变最大传输概率，最大传输概率由初始正能量分数限制，因此已经编码在Fock状态的相空间结构中。由于Fock状态无法在经典相空间中忠实地表示，因此通过屏障的传输揭示了半经典方法的根本局限性。


### Abstract

Transmission through potential barriers is a fundamental problem in quantum mechanics. While semiclassical methods can approximate certain aspects of transmission, they fail to capture the intrinsically quantum interference associated with Wigner-function negativity. We numerically study the transmission of displaced Fock states through an inverted-oscillator barrier, with and without a Kerr nonlinearity that offers a potential route to experimental realization. These states allow only an approximate classical description, since their characteristic Wigner-function negativity is absent in phase space. The semiclassical simulation reproduces the overall transmission but deviate from exact results and fail to capture short-time plateaus that arise when regions of Wigner-function negativity cross the barrier. With the Kerr nonlinearity, reflections from nonlinear boundaries drive interference into classically forbidden regions, an effect that is inaccessible to semiclassical approaches. We find that these interference effects do not alter the maximum transmission probability, which is bounded by the initial positive-energy fraction and therefore already encoded in the phase-space structure of the Fock states. Because Fock states cannot be faithfully represented within classical phase space, the transmission through a barrier reveals fundamental limitations of semiclassical approaches.


---


## 保持一致的端点工作准统计中的捷径错误签名

**Original Title:** Shortcut-error signatures in coherence-retaining endpoint work quasistatistics

**Authors:** Gabriella G. Damas, G. D. de Moraes Neto

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18095v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18095v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

量子功统计与经典功统计不同，因为初始能量一致性很重要。标准的两点测量（BPM）给出正分布，但会擦除相信息。保持一致的终点功准统计学提供了捷径到隔热性能的紧凑探测。对于相对于参考Hamilton量定义的功，精确的反热捷径将最终的参考Hamilton量拉回到初始能量基中的操作员对角线。端点Kirkwood-Dirac或Margenau-Hill准统计量随后失去对初始一致性的敏感性，并简化为BPM结果。不完美的捷径恢复了这种敏感性：非换相控制误差在误差幅度的一阶上产生偏离对角线的回拉Hamilton元素，而仅限种群的转移概率仅在二阶上改变。谐振子和量子位基准测试证实了这种线性与二次对比。该结果补充了包容性工作成本分析：它不测量辅助场的能量成本，但提供了残余非耐热性的相敏终点诊断。


### Abstract

Quantum work statistics differ from classical ones because initial energy coherence matters. The standard two-point measurement (TPM) gives a positive distribution but erases phase information. Coherence-retaining endpoint-work quasistatistics provide a compact probe of shortcut-to-adiabaticity performance. For work defined with respect to a reference Hamiltonian, an exact counterdiabatic shortcut pulls the final reference Hamiltonian back to an operator diagonal in the initial energy basis. Endpoint Kirkwood-Dirac or Margenau-Hill quasistatistics then lose sensitivity to initial coherence and reduce to the TPM result. Imperfect shortcuts restore this sensitivity: a non-commuting control error produces off-diagonal pulled-back Hamiltonian elements at first order in the error amplitude, whereas population-only transition probabilities change only at second order. Harmonic-oscillator and qubit benchmarks confirm this linear-versus-quadratic contrast. The result complements inclusive work-cost analyses: it does not measure the auxiliary field's energetic cost, but provides a phase-sensitive endpoint diagnostic of residual nonadiabaticity.


---


## 量子电池供电的几何Landau-Zener干涉术

**Original Title:** Quantum-Battery-Powered Geometric Landau-Zener Interferometry

**Authors:** Borhan Ahmadi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18108v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18108v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

经典的微波驱动器通常被视为用于超导量子位控制的理想相参功源。如果这样的驱动器被有限量子电池取代会怎样？作为一个要求严格的基准，我们考虑了由单个量化玻色子模式提供动力的回声重聚焦几何朗道-齐纳干涉测量法。量子位-电池动力学由杰恩斯-卡明斯汉密尔顿式描述，而回声脉冲则保留为纯量子位的重新聚焦操作，从而抵消了动力学阶段。在宏观相关状态极限下，恢复了通常的经典几何干涉仪。然而，在有限的平均量子数下，Jaynes-Cummings耦合产生了与间隙$«_n= 2g\squtt {n}$的子数解析避免的交叉。纯量子位的回声在相邻激发扇形之间重新分配幅度，因此有限电池协议不是单个经典干涉仪，而是一种连贯的扇形分辨量子进化。这会产生对比度损失、干涉图失真和可测量的电池反作用。我们进一步表明，仅仅减少量子数波动是不够的：几何控制需要一阶相参考。因此，几何朗道-齐纳干涉测量法为认证相连贯量子电池能量提供了实用的基准。


### Abstract

Classical microwave drives are usually treated as ideal phase-coherent work sources for superconducting-qubit control. What if such a drive is replaced by a finite quantum battery. As a demanding benchmark, we consider echo-refocused geometric Landau--Zener interferometry powered by a single quantized bosonic mode. The qubit--battery dynamics are described by a Jaynes--Cummings Hamiltonian, while the echo pulse is retained as a qubit-only refocusing operation that cancels the dynamical phase. In the macroscopic coherent-state limit, the usual classical geometric interferometer is recovered. At finite mean photon number, however, the Jaynes--Cummings coupling generates photon-number-resolved avoided crossings with gaps $Ω_n=2g\sqrt{n}$. The qubit-only echo redistributes amplitudes between neighboring excitation sectors, so the finite-battery protocol is not a single classical interferometer but a coherent sector-resolved quantum evolution. This produces contrast loss, interferogram distortions, and measurable battery back-action. We further show that reducing photon-number fluctuations alone is not sufficient: geometric control requires a first-order phase reference. Geometric Landau--Zener interferometry therefore provides a practical benchmark for certifying phase-coherent quantum-battery energy.


---


## 通过顺序测量对量子上下文进行线性光学测试

**Original Title:** Linear-optical test of quantum contextuality with sequential measurements

**Authors:** Jiaqi Liu, Bita Olamaei, Lijian Zhang, Ali Asadian, Saleh Rahimi-Keshari

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18112v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18112v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

量子上下文性提供了非经典行为的基本特征，而非上下文隐变量模型无法解释。我们提出并通过实验实现了一种线性光学装置，用于通过使用单量子违反KCBS不等式来演示Kochen-Specker上下文。我们的方案采用线性光学网络和开关光检测器实现的顺序测量。该结构确保每个共同测量的观察对象都通过不同上下文的相同物理操作来实现。我们的实验结果证明了KCBS不等式的明显违反以及对量子损失的鲁棒性。除了基本研究之外，拟议的设置还为探测量子状态的非经典性和量子数统计提供了一个实用工具，这反过来又可以验证单量子源。


### Abstract

Quantum contextuality provides a fundamental signature of nonclassical behavior that cannot be explained by noncontextual hidden-variable models. We propose and experimentally implement a linear-optical setup for demonstrating Kochen-Specker contextuality via a violation of the KCBS inequality using single photons. Our scheme employs sequential measurements realized with linear-optical networks and on-off photodetectors. The construction ensures that each co-measured observable is implemented by the same physical operation across different contexts. Our experimental results demonstrate a clear violation of the KCBS inequality and robustness against photon loss. Beyond fundamental investigations, the proposed setup provides a practical tool for probing non-classicality and photon-number statistics of quantum states, which in turn enables the verification of single-photon sources.

## 基于4 H-SiC微片的集成时间仓纠缠量子光源

**Original Title:** Integrated time-bin entangled quantum light source on a 4H-SiC microring chip

**Authors:** Hong Zeng, Bing-Cheng Yang, Yun-Ru Fan, Li-Ping Zhou, Cheng-Li Wang, Bo-Wen Chen, Ai-Lun Yi, Yong Geng, Guang-Wei Deng, You Wang, Hai-Zhi Song, Jun-Tao Zhang, Hao Li, Li-Xing You, Zi-Hao Zhan, Kai Guo, Xin Ou, Guang-Can Guo, Qiang Zhou

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18124v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18124v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

具有腔增强非线性光学过程的集成时元纠缠光对源对于量子信息技术至关重要。然而，具有高品质因子的微腔本质上会在产生效率和量子带宽之间引入权衡，这阻碍了具有集成光源的高速量子网络的发展。在这里，我们通过优化材料的非线性特性和具有4 H-碳化硅平台的集成微型谐振器的几何形状来解决这一挑战。该设备以1.9 $\x $105的负载质量因子工作，频谱带宽为1.0 GHz，并用间隔1.25 ns的300 ps双脉冲以160 MHz的重复率进行抽运，实现了时间面元纠缠光对产生率为1.35 $\x $107 s-1 MW-2。测量的原始可见度为95.55 $\PM $0.18%，表明违反贝尔不等式超过138个标准差，通过量子状态断层扫描获得的保真度为94.37 $\PM $0.22%。这些结果为高效和宽带时间点纠缠量子光源提供了可扩展的途径，克服了基于腔体的设计的固有限制，并为未来量子通信网络推进了集成平台。


### Abstract

Integrated time-bin-entangled photon-pair source with cavity-enhanced nonlinear optical processes is essential for quantum information technologies. However, microcavities with a high quality factor inherently introduce a trade-off between generation efficiency and photon bandwidth, which hinders the development of high-speed quantum networks with an integrated source. Here, we address this challenge by optimizing the nonlinearity property of the material and the geometry of the integrated microring resonator with a 4H-silicon carbide platform. Operating at a loaded quality factor of 1.9 $\times$ 10^5 - spectral bandwidth of 1.0 GHz and pumped with 300-ps double pulses separated by 1.25 ns at a repetition rate of 160 MHz, the device achieves a time-bin-entangled photon-pair generation rate of 1.35 $\times$ 10^7 s^-1 mW^-2. A raw visibility of 95.55 $\pm$ 0.18% is measured, showing a violation of Bell's inequality by more than 138 standard deviations, and a fidelity of 94.37 $\pm$ 0.22% is obtained by quantum state tomography. These results provide a scalable pathway to an efficient and broadband time-bin entangled quantum light source, overcoming intrinsic limitations of cavity-based designs and advancing integrated platforms for future quantum communication networks.

## 有限种群不平衡偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中的限制控制模式选择

**Original Title:** Confinement-controlled pattern selection in a finite population-imbalanced dipolar Bose-Einstein condensate

**Authors:** Zhenhao Wang, Weijing Bao, Jia-Rui Luo, Gentaro Watanabe, Kui-Tian Xi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18139v2

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18139v2

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

本文研究了一个准二维圆形盒子中粒子数不平衡的两分量偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体的基态密度分布。使用平均场模型，我们绘制出相图的轴向限制，相互作用的不平衡，和人口比例的函数。该系统支持一个丰富的序列的静态形态，包括一个几乎均匀的煎饼状态，煎饼液滴和环液滴共存状态，液滴阵列，和同心环。这些图案显示出与二嵌段共聚物系统中的微相分离形态的密切结构对应，其中群体不平衡充当选择图案拓扑结构的有效体积分数。对密度分布和结构因子的分析表明，调制状态具有固有的非零特征波矢，当盒子尺寸变化时，该特征波矢基本保持不变。我们还发现，特征图案间距与轴向限制长度呈线性关系，这表明凝结水的横向厚度控制着有效的面内长度尺度。在有限圆盒中，这种平滑的缩放被离散的步骤打断，反映了几何挫败和环或液滴数量的整定锁定。我们的结果表明，盒俘获偶极混合物为研究量子流体中的有限尺寸图案选择和非局部微相形成提供了一个可控平台。


### Abstract

We study the ground-state density patterns of a population-imbalanced two-component dipolar Bose-Einstein condensate confined in a circular quasi-two-dimensional box. Using a mean-field model, we map out phase diagrams as functions of the axial confinement, interaction imbalance, and population ratio. The system supports a rich sequence of stationary morphologies, including a nearly uniform pancake state, pancake-droplet and ring-droplet coexistence states, droplet arrays, and concentric rings. These patterns show a close structural correspondence to microphase-separated morphologies in diblock-copolymer systems, with the population imbalance acting as an effective volume fraction that selects the pattern topology. Analysis of the density profiles and structure factors reveals that the modulated states possess an intrinsic nonzero characteristic wave vector, which remains essentially unchanged when the box size is varied. We also find that the characteristic pattern spacing scales linearly with the axial confinement length, indicating that the transverse thickness of the condensate controls the effective in-plane length scale. In a finite circular box, this smooth scaling is interrupted by discrete steps, reflecting geometric frustration and the integer locking of the number of rings or droplets. Our results show that box-trapped dipolar mixtures provide a controllable platform for studying finite-size pattern selection and nonlocal microphase formation in quantum fluids.

## 多控制Toffoli门的测量驱动自适应低开销实现

**Original Title:** Measurement-Driven Adaptive Low-Overhead Implementation of Multi-Controlled Toffoli Gates

**Authors:** Abhoy Kole, Till Schnittka, Rolf Drechsler

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18159v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18159v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

Toffoli门是量子算术和可逆逻辑的基本构建模块，但其有效实现仍然是近期和耐故障量子架构中的一个重大挑战。动态量子电路能力的最新进展（包括中间电路测量和经典的前向）为减少非Clifford操作的资源负担提供了新的机会。   在这项工作中，我们提出了一套用于多控制Toffoli门的动态分解策略，这些策略利用自适应电路执行和辅助结构。与传统静态分解相比，我们的方法系统性地减少了纠缠门计数、T计数和T深度，同时保留了故障容忍保证。通过分析成本模型和实验评估，我们证明相对相基元和测量条件修正可以实现可扩展的实施，并提高深度和资源效率。


### Abstract

The Toffoli gate is a fundamental building block for quantum arithmetic and reversible logic, yet its efficient realization remains a major challenge in both near-term and fault-tolerant quantum architectures. Recent advances in dynamic quantum circuit capabilities, including mid-circuit measurement and classical feedforward, provide new opportunities for reducing the resource overhead of non-Clifford operations.
  In this work, we propose a set of dynamic decomposition strategies for multi-controlled Toffoli gates that exploit adaptive circuit execution and ancilla-assisted constructions. Our methods systematically reduce entangling-gate count, T-count, and T-depth compared with conventional static decompositions, while preserving fault-tolerance guarantees. Through analytical cost models and experimental evaluation, we demonstrate that relative-phase primitives and measurement-conditioned corrections enable scalable implementations with improved depth and resource efficiency.

## 具有一个干净的Ancilla的大型Toffoli门的自适应Clifford+T分解

**Original Title:** Adaptive Clifford+T Decomposition of Large Toffoli Gates with One Clean Ancilla

**Authors:** Abhoy Kole, Majd Assaad, Till Schnittka, Rolf Drechsler

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18169v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18169v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

多控制Toffoli门是量子计算的基本构建模块，应用于量子算术、模拟和搜索算法。在故障容忍架构中，它们的实现受到非Clifford资源高成本的限制，特别是在T计数和T深度方面。最近的进展表明，使用辅助量子位、相对相Toffoli门和动态电路技术可以大幅减少这种负担。   在这项工作中，我们研究了在存在单个干净辅助子和有条件干净辅助子的情况下使用3和4输入相对相Toffoli门对大型Toffoli门的分解。我们为Clifford+T实现推导出明确的资源边界，其中结合了基于动态电路的非计算和测量条件修正。我们的分析强调在固定CX和T计数费用下减少T深度，确保与近期设备的相关性。我们表明，引入4输入相对相Toffoli门可以通过增强并行性来显着降低T深度，同时保持有利的辅助要求。我们通过实验评估和与现有方法的比较分析进一步验证了我们的理论结果。


### Abstract

Multi-controlled Toffoli gates are fundamental building blocks in quantum computation, with applications in quantum arithmetic, simulation, and search algorithms. In fault-tolerant architectures, their realization is constrained by the high cost of non-Clifford resources, particularly in terms of T-count and T-depth. Recent advances have demonstrated that the use of ancillary qubits, relative-phase Toffoli gates, and dynamic circuit techniques can substantially reduce this overhead.
  In this work, we investigate the decomposition of large Toffoli gates using 3- and 4-input relative-phase Toffoli gates in the presence of a single clean ancilla and conditionally clean ancillas. We derive explicit resource bounds for Clifford+T implementations incorporating dynamic-circuit-based uncomputation and measurement-conditioned corrections. Our analysis emphasizes T-depth reduction under fixed CX and T-count overhead, ensuring relevance for near-term devices. We show that introducing 4-input relative-phase Toffoli gates enables significant T-depth reductions through enhanced parallelism while maintaining favorable ancilla requirements. We further validate our theoretical results through experimental evaluation and comparative analysis with existing approaches.

## 具有排斥核的有限范围吸引势有效范围的正性

**Original Title:** Positivity of the effective range for finite range attractive potentials with a repulsive core

**Authors:** Davide Germani

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18207v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18207v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

在奇异强子的唯象学研究中，有效范围的符号$r_0$被用作区分紧凑多强子配置（与$r_0 < 0$相关）和松散束缚强子分子（$r_0 > 0$）的标准。受此启发，我们研究了单通道局部相互作用有效范围符号的基本限制。我们严格证明，对于以内排斥核和外吸引尾为特征的有限范围势，只要散射长度大于势的范围（$a > R$），有效范围仍然严格为正。


### Abstract

In the phenomenological study of exotic hadrons, the sign of the effective range, $r_0$, is invoked as a criterion to distinguish between compact multiquark configurations (associated with $r_0 < 0$) and loosely bound hadronic molecules ($r_0 > 0$). Motivated by this, we investigate the fundamental constraints on the sign of the effective range for single-channel local interactions. We rigorously prove that for finite-range potentials, characterized by an inner repulsive core and an outer attractive tail, the effective range remains strictly positive provided that the scattering length is greater than the range of the potential ($a > R$).

## 毫开氏温度下，Eu $'{3+}$：CaWO$_4$的音素锁紧旋转松弛

**Original Title:** Phonon-bottlenecked spin relaxation of Er$^{3+}$:CaWO$_4$ at milliKelvin temperatures

**Authors:** S. Rajendran, B. Mistri, P. K. Sharma, S. E. Kubatkin, A. V. Danilov, S. Dhomkar, S. E. de Graaf, V. Ranjan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18208v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18208v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们研究了在毫克尔温温度下，通过耦合到低模体积超导共振器来检测电子旋转的旋转-格子驰豫时间。在支持强音素发射率的大磁场下，我们观察到随着旋转激发的增加，松弛时间显着增加，这表现出独特的$[\tanh（\hbar ω_0/k_\text{B} T）]' 2 $温度依赖性。这些观察结果是典型的音素交叉旋转松弛，并对利用稀土旋转系综作为相干资源的量子技术产生了影响。


### Abstract

We study spin-lattice relaxation times of electron spins in Er$^{3+}$:CaWO$_4$ at millikelvin temperature, detected via their coupling to a low-mode volume superconducting resonator. At large magnetic field supporting strong phonon-emission rates, we observe a noticeable increase in relaxation times with increasing spin-excitations, which exhibit a unique $[\tanh (\hbar ω_0/k_\text{B} T)]^2$ temperature dependence. These observations are typical of a phonon-bottlenecked spin relaxation, and have implications for quantum technologies that exploit rare-earth spin ensembles as coherent resources.

## 量子Rabi模型的规则反热驱动

**Original Title:** Regularized Counterdiabatic Driving for the Quantum Rabi Model

**Authors:** Julián Ferreiro-Vélez, Pablo García-Azorín, F. A. Cárdenas-López, Xi Chen

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18237v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18237v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

反非热（CD）驱动通过抑制有限时间进化期间的非热激发，提供了快速、稳健的状态准备的强大途径。然而，为复杂系统推导分析CD协议仍然具有挑战性，这激励了变分方法的发展。这些方法通常依赖于最小化基于轨迹的函式来构建近似控制Hamilton。然而，在无界系统中，由于无界玻色子希尔伯特空间，此类函元可能会变得不明确，从而导致不同的成本函数和非物理变分系数。在这里，我们介绍了一个变分优化框架，配备了物理动机的重整化方案，通过将其限制在相关的位移和低能量子空间来正则化基于迹的度量。作为一个典型的例子，我们将我们的方法应用到量子拉比模型超越色散近似，并确定两个不同的CD贡献耦合原子的自由度的位置和动量求积的字段。这些条款抑制非绝热激发耦合制度，从强到深强的光-物质相互作用。我们进一步制定了一个基于密度的量子最优控制策略，绕过了基于轨迹的变分方法的局限性。最后，我们表明，所产生的CD项可以通过Floquet工程通过原生Hamilton的参数调制来实现。我们的结果表明，CD驱动可以一致地扩展到具有无界Hilbert空间的连续变量系统，为强相互作用光物质平台中的量子控制提供受控且可扩展的框架。


### Abstract

Counter-diabatic (CD) driving provides a powerful route to fast and robust state preparation by suppressing diabatic excitations during finite-time evolution. Yet, deriving analytical CD protocols for complex systems remains challenging, motivating the development of variational approaches. These methods typically rely on minimizing trace-based functionals to construct approximate control Hamiltonians. However, in unbounded systems, such functionals can become ill-defined because of the unbounded bosonic Hilbert space, leading to divergent cost functions and unphysical variational coefficients. Here, we introduce a variational optimization framework equipped with physically motivated renormalization schemes that regularize the trace-based metric by restricting it to relevant displaced and low-energy subspaces. As a paradigmatic example, we apply our method to the quantum Rabi model beyond the dispersive approximation and identify two distinct CD contributions that couple the atomic degree of freedom to the position and momentum quadratures of the field. These terms suppress diabatic excitations across coupling regimes ranging from strong to deep-strong light--matter interaction. We further formulate a fidelity-based quantum optimal-control strategy that bypasses the limitations of trace-based variational methods. Finally, we show that the resulting CD terms can be implemented via Floquet engineering through parametric modulation of the native Hamiltonian. Our results demonstrate that CD driving can be consistently extended to continuous-variable systems with unbounded Hilbert spaces, providing a controlled and scalable framework for quantum control in strongly interacting light-matter platforms.


---


## 局部Hamilton上量子算法的熵控制加速

**Original Title:** An Entropy-Governed Speedup for Quantum Algorithms on Local Hamiltonians

**Authors:** Ranitha Mataraarachchi, François Le Gall, Suguru Tamaki

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18241v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18241v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

低能量估计和状态准备一般$k$-本地哈密顿量是量子复杂性理论的基本挑战。对于恒定的相对精度，Buhrman等人（PRL 2025）最近打破了自然Grover界$O（2^{n/2}）$，其中$n$表示量子比特的数量，对于这两个问题。在本文中，对于任何足够小的参数$d\ge 0$，我们提出了一个更快的量子算法，该算法输出的量子态的能量在所有深度$d$态上都以最小能量为界（即，通过对全零状态应用深度电路而获得的状态），以及该能量的估计。对于深度为-$d$的Hamilton类，我们的算法进一步实现了与Buhrman等人完全相同的能量保证。我们的结果还深入了解了强纠缠状态和允许有效经典描述的状态之间的区别。


### Abstract

Low-energy estimation and state preparation for general $k$-local Hamiltonians are fundamental challenges in quantum complexity theory. For constant relative accuracy, Buhrman et al. (PRL 2025) recently broke the natural Grover bound $O(2^{n/2})$, where $n$ denotes the number of qubits, for both problems. In this paper, for any sufficiently small parameter $d\ge 0$, we present an even faster quantum algorithm that outputs a quantum state with energy bounded by the minimum energy over all depth-$d$ states (i.e., states obtained by applying a depth-$d$ circuit to the all-zero state), together with an estimate of this energy. For the class of Hamiltonians with depth-$d$ ground states, our algorithm furthermore achieves exactly the same energy guarantees as Buhrman et al. Our results also provide insight into the distinction between strongly entangled states and those admitting efficient classical descriptions.


---


## 一个纯转向状态意味着爱因斯坦-波多尔斯基-罗森转向

**Original Title:** One pure steered state implies Einstein-Podolsky-Rosen steering

**Authors:** Qiu-Cheng Song, Joonwoo Bae

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18243v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18243v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

在这项工作中，我们证明了一个两量子比特纠缠态至少允许一个纯转向态是爱因斯坦-波多尔斯基-罗森（EPR）可控从爱丽丝到鲍勃。纯转向态意味着鲍勃的量子转向椭球至少在一点上与他的布洛赫球相切。此外，我们还证明了对于两个量子比特的纠缠态，Bob的量子转向椭球与其Bloch球相切于N个点，当且仅当Alice的量子转向椭球与其Bloch球相切于N个点.因此，对于任何两量子比特纠缠态，如果一方可以将另一方引导到至少一个纯态，则该状态是双向EPR可操纵的。我们还提出了两量子位纠缠态的几个启发性例子，以便可以根据纯操纵状态来验证EPR操纵。我们的结果解决了EPR转向场景中的吉辛定理：至少一个纯转向状态意味着双向转向。


### Abstract

In this work, we show that a two-qubit entangled state admitting at least one pure steered state is Einstein-Podolsky-Rosen (EPR) steerable from Alice to Bob. Pure steered states signifies that the quantum steering ellipsoid of Bob is tangent to his Bloch sphere at least at a single point. Furthermore, we prove that for a two-qubit entangled state, Bob's quantum steering ellipsoid is tangent to his Bloch sphere at exactly $N$ points, for $N\in \{ 0,1,2,\infty\}$, if and only if Alice's quantum steering ellipsoid is tangent to her Bloch sphere at exactly $N$ points. For any two-qubit entangled state, therefore, if one party can steer the other to at least one pure state, the state is two-way EPR steerable. We also present several illuminating instances of two-qubit entangled states such that the EPR steering can be verified in terms of pure steered states. Our result addresses the Gisin theorem in a EPR steering scenario: at least a single pure steered state implies two-way steering.


---


## 非相对论性旋转-$\fRAC{1}{2}$粒子系统的量子-流体对应

**Original Title:** Quantum--Fluid Correspondence for Systems of Nonrelativistic Spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ Particles

**Authors:** Naoki Sato, Michio Yamada

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18247v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18247v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们表明，被赋予内部旋转自由度的带电流体自然满足非相对论性旋转1/2粒子的泡利方程，并且n个这样的相互作用流体的集合可以重新表达为3 n维的欧拉流，从而提供了n个泡利粒子系统的自然表示。这些结果提供了泡利方程的流体力学推导，并将马德隆（量子流体动力学）图像扩展到多粒子量子系统。特别是，它们意味着n量子位量子计算机至少在原则上可以被实现为n种流体的适当组合，或等效地被实现为3 n维欧拉流。


### Abstract

We show that a charged fluid endowed with an internal spin degree of freedom naturally satisfies the Pauli equation for a nonrelativistic spin-1/2 particle, and that a collection of n such interacting fluids can be reformulated as an Euler flow in 3n dimensions, thereby providing a natural representation of a system of n Pauli particles. These results provide a fluid-mechanical derivation of the Pauli equation and extend the Madelung, or quantum-hydrodynamic, picture to many-particle quantum systems. In particular, they imply that an n-qubit quantum computer can, at least in principle, be realized as a suitable combination of n fluids, or equivalently as a 3n-dimensional Euler flow.

## 1-D和2-D非厄米特皮肤效应的能量分辨本征模光谱

**Original Title:** Energy-Resolved Eigenmode Spectroscopy of 1-D and 2-D Non-Hermitian Skin Effects

**Authors:** Rohith Srikanth, Sashank Kaushik Sridhar, Avik Dutt

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18272v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18272v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

非埃尔米特格子可以承受非埃尔米特集肤效应，即边界诱导的所有体本征态坍缩为指数局部边缘模式。这种效应是异常体边界对应和非厄米派传感显着增强的基础，但对非厄米派格子本征模的直接能量分辨访问仍然有限。在这里，我们报告了频率合成维度中皮肤模式的能带和能量分辨本征模光谱。通过在电光学调制环形谐振器中引入强频域边界，我们实现了有限的非厄米特格子，并使用激光去调谐作为有效汉密尔顿量本征能量的光谱轴。然后，点分辨的频差测量重建每个模式的空间轮廓，揭示整个光谱中的边界局部皮肤状态及其与边缘的本征能量相关的位移。除了1D之外，相同的频率边界架构在有限网格之间结合远程耦合后，会产生真正的2D频率网格，而不是迄今为止在扭曲管上实现的折叠1D系统。在这些网格中，我们观察到两个合成维度中的可调定向传输和边缘定位。我们的结果引入了本征模谱作为非厄米特物理学的直接探测，并建立了强有界频率格子作为汉密尔顿工程的灵活平台。


### Abstract

Non-Hermitian lattices can host the non-Hermitian skin effect, a boundary-induced collapse of all bulk eigenstates into exponentially localized edge modes. This effect underlies anomalous bulk-boundary correspondence and remarkable enhancements in non-Hermitian sensing, yet direct energy-resolved access to the eigenmodes of non-Hermitian lattices has remained limited. Here we report band- and energy-resolved eigenmode spectroscopy of skin modes in a frequency synthetic dimension. By introducing strong frequency-domain boundaries in an electro-optically modulated ring resonator, we realize finite non-Hermitian lattices and use laser detuning as a spectroscopic axis for the eigenenergies of the effective Hamiltonian. Site-resolved heterodyne measurements then reconstruct the spatial profile of each mode, revealing boundary-localized skin states throughout the spectrum and their eigenenergy-dependent displacement from the edge. Beyond 1D, the same frequency-boundary architecture, upon incorporating long-range couplings between finite lattices, produces genuine 2D frequency lattices rather than the hitherto-realized folded 1D systems on twisted tubes. In these lattices we observe tunable directional transport and edge localization in two synthetic dimensions. Our results introduce eigenmode spectroscopy as a direct probe of non-Hermitian physics and establish strongly bounded frequency lattices as a flexible platform for Hamiltonian engineering.


---


## 腔光学力学引起的强纳米机械Duffing非线性和相互作用

**Original Title:** Strong nanomechanical Duffing nonlinearity and interactions induced through cavity optomechanics

**Authors:** Jesse J. Slim, Ewold Verhagen

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18289v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18289v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

非线性是经典和量子信号处理中的关键资源。非线性纳米机械元件的应用范围从传感到计算，而非线性共振器网络以及线性共振器的非线性耦合网络构成了模拟复杂动力学的有前途的平台。在这里，我们通过实验证明了一种在纳米机械共振器中实现强机械非线性的方法，该共振器通过光学激光驱动器完全控制。该机制利用腔光机系统中辐射-压力相互作用的非线性，从而产生非线性光学弹簧效应。由此产生的Duffing非线性可以通过泵激激光功率方便地调节强度，而其符号则由激光失调控制。此外，我们证明非线性光学弹簧调节了耦合到公共腔的机械模式之间的有效相互作用，从而在它们之间引发可调的非线性相互作用，从而影响光谱响应和动力学。这些结果将腔光学力学确立为一个通用的、现场可重新配置的平台，用于在共振器和网络中进行工程非线性动力学。


### Abstract

Nonlinearity is a key resource in both classical and quantum signal processing. Nonlinear nanomechanical elements have found applications ranging from sensing to computing, while networks of nonlinear resonators, as well as nonlinearly coupled networks of linear resonators, constitute promising platforms for simulating complex dynamics. Here, we experimentally demonstrate an approach to realizing strong mechanical nonlinearity in nanomechanical resonators, fully controlled through optical laser drives. The mechanism exploits the nonlinearity of the radiation-pressure interaction in a cavity optomechanical system, which gives rise to a nonlinear optical spring effect. The resulting Duffing nonlinearity is conveniently tunable in strength via pump laser power, while its sign is controlled by laser detuning. Moreover, we demonstrate that the nonlinear optical spring mediates effective interactions between mechanical modes coupled to a common cavity, inducing tunable nonlinear interactions between them that impact spectral response and dynamics. These results establish cavity optomechanics as a versatile and in-situ reconfigurable platform for engineering nonlinear dynamics in resonators and networks.


---


## 超越投影测量的量子随机性

**Original Title:** Quantum randomness beyond projective measurements

**Authors:** Fionnuala Curran

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18291v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18291v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

量子物理学的不可预测性导致了内在的随机性。在对抗场景中，任何额外的自由度都必须归因于与测量设置相关的窃听者。然后，通过她正确猜测测量结果的概率来量化真正的随机性，并对所有可能的策略进行优化。极端测量在这里很有吸引力，因为它们不允许信息泄露给这样的窃听者。然而，除了投影测量之外，还有一个简单的问题仍然悬而未决：给定的极端测量可以产生多少内在随机性？在解决这个问题的一个步骤中，我们对作用于任何状态的任何无偏极一级测量产生的随机性进行了量化，在二维中显式地解决了这个问题。这种类型的四个结果量子位测量是断层扫描的，因此这些结果也适用于完全依赖于源设备的随机性。我们发现，四面体对称信息完全（SIC）测量在这一类中具有最小的内在随机性。我们还提出了倾斜的SIC测量系列，并使用它们来部分解决一个悬而未决的问题：我们证明了$2 \log d$比特的随机性（最大数量）可以在存在SIC测量的任何维度中根据设备依赖（或源设备独立）生成。


### Abstract

The unpredictability of quantum physics gives rise to intrinsic randomness. In an adversarial scenario, any additional degrees of freedom must be attributed to an eavesdropper with correlations to the measurement set-up. The true randomness is then quantified by the probability that she correctly guesses the measurement outcomes, optimised over all possible strategies. Extremal measurements are appealing here, since they do not allow information to leak to such an eavesdropper. Beyond projective measurements, however, a simple question remains open: how much intrinsic randomness can be generated by a given extremal measurement? In a step towards solving it, we characterise the randomness generated by any unbiased extremal rank-one measurement acting on any state, solving the problem explicitly in dimension two. Four-outcome qubit measurements of this type are tomographic, so these results hold for fully source-device-dependent randomness too. The tetrahedral symmetric informationally complete (SIC) measurement, we find, has the least intrinsic randomness within this class. We also present the skewed SIC family of measurements, and use them to partially solve an open problem: we prove that $2 \log d$ bits of randomness, the maximal amount, can be generated device-dependently (or source-device-independently) in any dimension in which there exists a SIC measurement.


---


## QLIF-cast：用于时间序列天气预报的量子泄漏集成和火灾

**Original Title:** QLIF-CAST: Quantum Leaky-Integrate-and-Fire for Time-Series Weather Forecasting

**Authors:** Alberto Marchisio, Aayan Ebrahim, Nouhaila Innan, Muhammad Kashif, Muhammad Shafique

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18333v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18333v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

准确有效的时间序列预测对于经典和量子神经架构来说仍然是一个具有挑战性的问题，特别是在多元环境中。这项工作将Quantum Leaky Integrate-and-Fire（QLily）尖峰神经网络改编为时间序列回归任务，特别是短期多元天气预报。我们将Qinf扩展到分类之外，并证明其对连续值预测问题的适用性。   QLIF-AST模型将神经元激发状态编码为单量子位量子叠加，由Rx旋转门和T1松弛衰变驱动，并嵌入在混合量子经典循环架构中。我们进行两种不同的评估。首先，与多元天气数据集参数匹配的经典Lily基线进行的对照比较显示，QLIF-AST的SSE降低了15.4%，MAE降低了4.4%，这表明量子神经元动力学比经典等效物减少了预测误差。其次，对空气质量和风速基准进行的最先进的量子LSTM（QLSTM）和量子神经网络（QNN）模型的跨领域比较分析表明，QLIF-UTE收敛的训练时间减少了高达94%，在速度误差权衡空间中占据了独特的位置。IBM马拉喀什（156量子位QPU）上的硬件验证证实了可靠的电路执行，与模拟的平均偏差仅为1.2%。


### Abstract

Accurate and efficient time-series forecasting remains a challenging problem for both classical and quantum neural architectures, particularly in multivariate environmental settings. This work adapts the Quantum Leaky Integrate-and-Fire (QLIF) spiking neural network for time-series regression tasks, specifically short-term multivariate weather forecasting. We extend QLIF beyond classification and demonstrate its applicability to continuous-valued prediction problems.
  The QLIF-CAST model encodes neuron excitation states as single-qubit quantum superpositions, driven by Rx rotation gates and T1 relaxation decay, and is embedded within a hybrid quantum-classical recurrent architecture. We conduct two distinct evaluations. First, a controlled comparison against a parameter-matched classical LIF baseline on a multivariate weather dataset shows that QLIF-CAST achieves 15.4% lower MSE and 4.4% lower MAE, demonstrating that quantum neuronal dynamics reduce prediction error over classical equivalents. Second, a cross-domain comparative analysis with state-of-the-art quantum LSTM (QLSTM) and quantum neural network (QNN) models on air quality and wind speed benchmarks reveals that QLIF-CAST converges in up to 94% less training time, occupying a distinct position in the speed-error trade-off space. Hardware verification on IBM Marrakesh (156-qubit QPU) confirms reliable circuit execution with only 1.2% average deviation from simulation.

## 混合量子-经典神经架构搜索

**Original Title:** Hybrid Quantum-Classical Neural Architecture Search

**Authors:** Alberto Marchisio, Muhammad Kashif, Nouhaila Innan, Muhammad Shafique

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18345v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18345v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

混合量子-经典神经网络（HQNN）正在成为嘈杂的中等规模量子（NISQ）时代量子机器学习的实用方法，因为它们将经典学习组件与参数化量子电路结合在端到端可训练框架中。然而，它们的性能和效率在很大程度上取决于架构选择，例如数据编码、电路结构、测量设计以及经典模块和量子模块之间的耦合。这使得手动设计变得越来越困难，尤其是当还必须考虑硬件限制和资源限制时。在本文中，我们研究了HQNN和神经架构搜索（NAS）的基础，讨论了NAS如何扩展到量子和混合设置，并演示了FLOPs感知搜索（其中FLOPs充当计算复杂性的代理），作为构建HQNN的重要硬件感知方向，不仅准确，而且计算效率高且可实际部署。


### Abstract

Hybrid quantum-classical neural networks (HQNNs) are emerging as a practical approach for quantum machine learning in the noisy intermediate-scale quantum (NISQ) era, as they combine classical learning components with parameterized quantum circuits in an end-to-end trainable framework. However, their performance and efficiency depend strongly on architectural choices such as data encoding, circuit structure, measurement design, and the coupling between classical and quantum modules. This makes manual design increasingly difficult, especially when hardware limitations and resource constraints must also be taken into account. In this paper, we study the foundations of HQNNs and neural architecture search (NAS), discuss how NAS extends to quantum and hybrid settings, and demonstrate FLOPs-aware search (where FLOPs serve as a proxy for computational complexity), as an important hardware-aware direction for building HQNNs that are not only accurate but also computationally efficient and practically deployable.
