## Zeno辅助量子热力发动机

**Original Title:** Zeno-Assisted Quantum Heat Engines

**Authors:** Selma Memić, Rafael Wagner, Susana F. Huelga, Martin B. Plenio

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18367v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18367v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

延时量子热力发动机（QHE）通常比准静态量子热力发动机提取的功少，因为快速驱动会在工作行程期间产生内聚和非隔热转变，这种现象通常称为量子摩擦。量子润滑指的是使用辅助系统或控制来减轻这种损失的一类广泛策略。在这项工作中，我们引入了一种基于量子Zeno动力学（QWD）的润滑协议。通过将工作媒体与辅助润滑系统连接并频繁监测润滑剂，我们将关节演变限制在Zeno子空间，并在运行Otto循环的QHE的工作行程期间获得隔热性的有效捷径。在理想的Zeno极限下，该协议再现了在瞬时能量基础上保留种群并在有限的中风持续时间恢复奥托效率所需的无过渡动态。我们还分析了几种与实施相关的热力学成本，包括切换、驱动、监控和不完美热化，以评估这些成本如何限制效率和功率的实际收益。我们的结果将QZZ确定为一种概念上不同的量子润滑途径，并强调量子热力机是研究强耦合、测量和量子热力学控制之间相互作用的有用环境。


### Abstract

Finite-time quantum heat engines (QHEs) typically extract less work than their quasistatic counterparts because fast driving generates coherences and non-adiabatic transitions during the work strokes, a phenomenon commonly referred to as quantum friction. Quantum lubrication denotes a broad class of strategies that use auxiliary systems or controls to mitigate this loss. In this work, we introduce a lubrication protocol based on the quantum Zeno dynamics (QZD). By coupling the working medium to an auxiliary lubricant system and frequently monitoring the lubricant, we confine the joint evolution to a Zeno subspace and obtain an effective shortcut to adiabaticity during the work strokes of a QHE running an Otto cycle. In the ideal Zeno limit, the protocol reproduces the transitionless dynamics required to preserve populations in the instantaneous energy basis and recover the Otto efficiency at finite stroke duration. We also analyze several implementation-dependent thermodynamic costs, including switching, driving, monitoring, and imperfect thermalization, in order to assess how these costs constrain the practical gains in efficiency and power. Our results identify QZD as a conceptually distinct route to quantum lubrication and highlight quantum heat engines as a useful setting in which to study the interplay between strong coupling, measurement, and quantum thermodynamic control.


---


## 超导电路中Floquet-Laughlin态的扩散辅助制备

**Original Title:** Dissipation-assisted preparation of Floquet-Laughlin states in superconducting circuits

**Authors:** Luis C. Steinfadt, André Eckardt, Francesco Petiziol

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18377v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18377v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

分数Chern绝缘体（FCI）是分数量子霍尔系统的格子类似物，其中强相互作用与受挫折隧道动力学的相互作用导致出现具有远程纠缠和任意子激发的有间隙的接地状态。此类系统的高度相关性使得其隔热制备的挑战性已经超出了两个颗粒的最小系统尺寸。考虑到超导电路中少数量子的玻色子Harper-Hofstadter-Hubbard模型的Floquet实现，我们设计了通过量子浴工程在半填充时FCI接地状态的驱动-消散稳定化的协议。通过与驱动漏腔模式的耦合来实现消散控制，从而实现了以Floquet-FCI作为其大致固定点的可调谐人工环境。对于由两个、三个和六个粒子组成的系统，我们用数字方式展示了控制方案的灵活性如何进一步允许在稳定的稳态中检测分数量子霍尔特征，包括体不可压缩性、霍尔响应和分数电荷的捕获。我们的结果为量子模拟器中的强相关状态的消散辅助制备提供了一条具体途径。


### Abstract

Fractional Chern insulators (FCIs) are lattice analogs of fractional quantum Hall systems, where the interplay of strong interactions with a frustrated tunnelling kinetics leads to the emergence of a gapped ground state with long-range entanglement and anyonic excitations. The highly correlated nature of such systems makes their adiabatic preparation challenging already beyond the minimal system size of two particles. Considering Floquet implementations of the bosonic Harper-Hofstadter-Hubbard model of few photons in superconducting circuits, we design protocols for the driven-dissipative stabilization of its FCI ground state at half filling via quantum bath engineering. Dissipation control is achieved through the coupling to driven leaky cavity modes, which realize a tuneable artificial environment having the Floquet-FCI as its approximate fixed point. For systems of two, three and six particles, we show numerically how the flexibility of the control scheme further allows for the detection of fractional quantum Hall signatures in the stabilized steady states, including bulk incompressibility, Hall response and the trapping of fractional charges. Our results provide a concrete pathway to dissipation-assisted preparation of strongly correlated states in quantum simulators.


---


## 随机通道不确定性下隐蔽量子通信的风险意识框架

**Original Title:** A Risk-Aware Framework for Covert Quantum Communication under Stochastic Channel Uncertainty

**Authors:** Abbas Arghavani, Shahid Raza, Maryam Amiri, Alessandro Papadopoulos

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18928v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18928v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

隐蔽量子通信（CQC）不仅寻求隐藏消息内容，还寻求隐藏通信的存在。现有的CQC模型通常假设确定性或最坏情况的通道条件，这在受湍流、波动背景辐射和随机检测器噪音影响的现实自由空间光学和量子链路中很难证明。我们提出了一个不确定物理层条件下的CQC随机风险感知优化框架。通过将传输率和背景噪音建模为随机变量，我们通过机会约束表达了隐蔽性和可靠性保证，并具有显式的停电预算$e_{cov}$和$e_{rel}}$。这将CQC设计重新定义为一个经过风险校准的资源分配问题，平衡吞吐量、隐蔽性、可靠性和通信隐私。我们推导出停电约束的基于分位的重新公式，描述随机不确定性下的可行运行区域，并引入补充的风险调整公用事业公式来揭示吞吐量-风险权衡。分析表明，在可接受的覆盖中断风险下进行适度放松可以产生大的吞吐量收益，而积极的优化可能会打破稀疏传输机制之外的隐蔽性。log正态衰落和随机热噪音下的蒙特卡罗结果表明，该框架扩展了可行操作区域，将隐蔽吞吐量提高了一个数量级以上，并确定了降级边界，超出该边界隐藏操作将变得不可靠。这些结果使CQC更接近现实的安全量子网络，用于自由空间、卫星和低检测概率应用。


### Abstract

Covert quantum communication (CQC) seeks to hide not only message content but also the existence of communication. Existing CQC models usually assume deterministic or worst-case channel conditions, which are difficult to justify in realistic free-space optical and quantum links affected by turbulence, fluctuating background radiance, and stochastic detector noise. We propose a stochastic risk-aware optimization framework for CQC under uncertain physical-layer conditions. By modeling transmissivity and background noise as random variables, we express covertness and reliability guarantees through chance constraints with explicit outage budgets $ε_{\text{cov}}$ and $ε_{\text{rel}}$. This recasts CQC design as a risk-calibrated resource-allocation problem balancing throughput, covertness, reliability, and communication privacy. We derive quantile-based reformulations of the outage constraints, characterize feasible operating regions under stochastic uncertainty, and introduce a complementary risk-adjusted utility formulation to expose throughput-risk trade-offs. The analysis reveals that modest relaxations in acceptable covertness-outage risk can yield large throughput gains, while aggressive optimization may break covertness outside sparse-transmission regimes. Monte Carlo results under log-normal fading and stochastic thermal noise show that the framework expands feasible operating regions, improves covert throughput by more than an order of magnitude, and identifies degradation boundaries beyond which covert operation becomes unreliable. These results move CQC closer to realistic secure quantum networking for free-space, satellite, and low-probability-of-detection applications.


---


## 简化状态稳定器雷尼（Rényi）信息量作为横向ANNNI模型和量子指南针模型中量子临界性的探索

**Original Title:** Reduced-State Stabilizer Rényi Entropy as a Probe of Quantum Criticality in the Transverse ANNNI Model and the Quantum Compass Model

**Authors:** Santanu Sarkar, George Biswas, Jun-Yi Wu, Anindya Biswas

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18391v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18391v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们研究了稳定器Rényi Entity（SRE）作为量子相转变指标的有效性，它是一个与非稳定器资源（量子魔法）相关的量化器。具体来说，我们分析了两个一维旋转模型（横向轴次近邻伊辛（TANNNI）模型和量子罗盘模型（QCM））的底价中约化密度矩阵的纯度修正SRE的行为。TANNNI模型的底薪是使用精确对角化技术获得的，而QCM是使用Jordan-Wigner（JW）变换分析的，然后对所得的二次费米子Hamilton进行Bogoliubov对角化。对于TANNNI模型，纯度修正的SRE成功地检测到高挫败区中的反相-浮动相转变，而在低挫败区中，原始（未经纯度修正的）SRE更准确地再现了已知的铁磁-顺磁相边界。对于QCM，纯度修正的SRE在各向同性点\（J_x/J_z=1\）附近表现出明显的特征，在该点处系统经历了一级量子相转变。我们的结果将约化状态的SRE确立为量子临界性的补充探测器，并进一步深入了解非稳定剂资源在多体量子相转变中的作用。


### Abstract

We investigate the effectiveness of the stabilizer Rényi entropy (SRE), a quantifier associated with non-stabilizer resources (quantum magic), as an indicator of quantum phase transitions. Specifically, we analyze the behavior of the purity-corrected SRE of reduced density matrices in the ground states of two one-dimensional spin models: the transverse axial next-nearest-neighbor Ising (TANNNI) model and the quantum compass model (QCM). The ground state of the TANNNI model is obtained using exact diagonalization techniques, while the QCM is analyzed using the Jordan--Wigner (JW) transformation followed by Bogoliubov diagonalization of the resulting quadratic fermionic Hamiltonian. For the TANNNI model, the purity-corrected SRE successfully detects the antiphase--floating phase transition in the high-frustration regime, while in the low-frustration regime the raw (purity-uncorrected) SRE reproduces the known ferromagnetic--paramagnetic phase boundaries more accurately. For the QCM, the purity-corrected SRE exhibits a clear signature near the isotropic point \(J_x/J_z=1\), where the system undergoes a first-order quantum phase transition. Our results establish SRE of reduced states as a complementary probe of quantum criticality and provide further insight into the role of non-stabilizer resources in many-body quantum phase transitions.


---


## 马尔可夫噪声下含时量子计量学的精度极限

**Original Title:** Precision limits for time-dependent quantum metrology under Markovian noise

**Authors:** Luca Previdi, Francesco Albarelli

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18392v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18392v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们推导出在存在一般马尔科夫噪音的情况下估计以{时间相关} Hamilton体编码的参数的最终精度界限，从而允许具有快速控制和无噪音辅助装置的任意自适应协议。将最小化过度纯化框架扩展到时变连续通道，我们获得了可实现的量子费舍尔信息（QFI）的差异上界，该信息可以通过半定规划随时进行评估。对于与参数无关的噪音，我们证明了一个普遍的长期标度定律：如果一致（无噪音）动态产生$Q_{\mathrm{coh}}（T）\sim T^{2k}$，那么在马尔科夫噪音下，QFI在DHNLS机制中最多缩放为$Q（T）\sim T^{2k}$，而在DHLS机制中，它从根本上限制为$Q（T）\sim T^{2k-1}$。我们在范式驱动量子位传感器上说明了这些行为，分别展示了去相和自发发射下的$T #{4}$和$T #{3}$缩放。最后，我们提供了显式的连续精确和近似量子误差修正构造--辅之以旋转压缩探针--它渐进地饱和界限，建立其紧密性。


### Abstract

We derive ultimate precision bounds for estimating parameters encoded in \emph{time-dependent} Hamiltonians in the presence of general Markovian noise, allowing for arbitrary adaptive protocols with fast controls and noiseless ancillas. Extending the minimization-over-purifications framework to time-varying continuous channels, we obtain a differential upper bound on the achievable quantum Fisher information (QFI) that can be evaluated at all times via semidefinite programming. For parameter-independent noise, we prove a universal long-time scaling law: if the coherent (noiseless) dynamics yields $Q_{\mathrm{coh}}(T)\sim T^{2k}$, then under Markovian noise the QFI scales at most as $Q(T)\sim T^{2k}$ in the DHNLS regime, whereas in the DHLS regime it is fundamentally limited to $Q(T)\sim T^{2k-1}$. We illustrate these behaviors on paradigmatic driven-qubit sensors, exhibiting $T^{4}$ and $T^{3}$ scalings under dephasing and spontaneous emission, respectively. Finally, we provide explicit continuous exact and approximate quantum error correction constructions -- supplemented by spin-squeezed probes -- that asymptotically saturate the bounds, establishing their tightness.


---


## CVRPTW的量子模型

**Original Title:** Quantum Model for CVRPTW

**Authors:** Imran Meghazi, Éric Bourreau

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18393v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18393v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

基于Grover Search框架，提出了一种求解带时间窗口容量车辆路径问题（CVRPTW）的量子算法。邮政服务在包裹递送或其他时间敏感的操作中经常面临这个问题。我们在基于门的量子计算机上提供了受经典路线优先、集群第二技术启发的模型的实现。量子范式允许克服这种分解的次优性固有属性。在当前的NISQ（Noisy Intermediate-Scale Quantum）时代，最重要的限制是可用量子位的数量，这使得时间窗口和容量限制难以解决。我们引入了一种量子比特高效的分裂启发模型，该模型仅向旅行推销员问题（TBC）的标准量子公式中添加线性数量的决策量子比特。


### Abstract

This paper proposes a quantum algorithm for the capacitated vehicle routing problem with time windows (CVRPTW) based on Grover Search framework. This problem is often faced by Postal services in the context of package delivery or other time-sensitive operations. We provide an implementation on gate based quantum computer of a model inspired by classical route first, cluster second technique. The quantum paradigm allows to overcome suboptimality inherent property of this decomposition. In the current NISQ (Noisy Intermediate-Scale Quantum) era, the most important limitation is the number of available qubits which makes time windows and capacity constraints hard to tackle. We introduce a qubit-efficient split-inspired modeling which adds only a linear number of decision qubits to standard quantum formulations for Traveling Salesman Problem (TSP).

## 驱动-消散玻色子链稳态中的地形保护长期相关性

**Original Title:** Topologically protected long-range correlations in steady states of driven-dissipative bosonic chains

**Authors:** Miguel Clavero Rubio, Tomás Ramos, Diego Porras

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18394v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18394v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

驱动耗散量子系统可以在拓扑机制中表现出鲁棒的传输和放大，但拓扑结构和相关程度之间的联系在很大程度上仍未被探索。在这项工作中，我们开发了一个通用的框架，通过奇异值分解（SVD）的驱动耗散系统的拓扑相玻色子相关。在本质上，我们声称，非厄米拓扑在二次刘维直接编码的稳态相关性，提供了一个内在的表征拓扑结构，而无需外部探针。我们发现，拓扑放大诱导无序鲁棒长程有序（LRO）在稳态相关性在固定频率，建立频率分辨的相关性作为非厄米拓扑相位的直接签名。我们引入了一个矢值的拓扑不变量，它捕获了频率轴上奇异值间隙闭合的总数，将隔热变形的概念从拓扑绝缘体扩展到二次刘维利安的拓扑相的情况。在这个框架内，我们进一步证明，等时相关性的空间结构编码了全局拓扑信息，表现为在拓扑阶段随距离的高斯空间衰减，与平凡阶段的指数衰减特征形成鲜明对比。这些发现为非埃尔米特系统中的量子传感和相关工程开辟了新的途径，并在俘获离子和超导电路等平台上实现了可行的实现。


### Abstract

Driven-dissipative quantum systems can exhibit robust transport and amplification in topological regimes, yet the connection between topology and the extent of correlations remains largely unexplored. In this work, we develop a general framework that links topological phases in driven-dissipative systems to bosonic correlations via the singular value decomposition (SVD). In essence, we claim that non-Hermitian topology in quadratic Liouvillians is directly encoded in steady-state correlations, providing an intrinsic characterization of topology without external probes. We show that topological amplification induces disorder-robust long-range order (LRO) in steady-state correlations at fixed frequency, establishing frequency-resolved correlations as direct signatures of non-Hermitian topological phases. We introduce a vector-valued topological invariant that captures the total number of singular-value gap closings across the frequency axis, extending the concept of adiabatic deformation from topological insulators to the case of topological phases of quadratic Liouvillians. Within this framework, we further demonstrate that the spatial structure of equal-time correlations encodes global topological information, manifested as a Gaussian spatial decay with distance in the topological phase, in contrast to the exponential decay characteristic of trivial phases. These findings open new avenues for quantum sensing and correlation engineering in non-Hermitian systems, with feasible implementations in platforms such as trapped ions and superconducting circuits.

## 成对纠缠网络中量子会议密钥协议的界限

**Original Title:** Bounds on quantum conference key agreement in pair-entangled networks

**Authors:** Justus Neumann, Hermann Kampermann, Dagmar Bruß, Anton Trushechkin

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18399v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18399v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们研究了短期量子网络中会议密钥协议的任务，其中节点通过双方纠缠态源连接，在不需要量子存储的局部操作类别下。我们根据网络布局和源的纠缠程度推导出可搜索会议密钥的上限，并证明这些界限在某些特定情况下的严格性。在这些情况下，我们表明，成对的双方密钥蒸馏，然后将双方密钥合并到会议密钥中是最佳的。


### Abstract

We investigate the task of conference key agreement in near-term quantum networks, where the nodes are connected by sources of bipartite entangled states, under the class of local operations not requiring quantum memory. We derive upper bounds on the distillable conference key depending on the network topology and degree of entanglement of the sources, and prove tightness of these bounds for some particular cases. In these cases, we show that pairwise bipartite key distillation followed by merging the bipartite keys into the conference key is optimal.

## 无质量粒子任意洛伦兹变换维格纳角的几何推导

**Original Title:** Geometrical derivation of Wigner's angle for arbitrary Lorentz transformations of massless particles

**Authors:** Isabella Cerutti, Petra F. Scudo

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18440v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18440v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

本注释总结了无质量粒子（特别是量子）洛伦兹变换的物理和数学。我们提供了维格纳小群矩阵的完整分析推导和任意洛伦兹变换的维格纳角计算的封闭公式。我们的推导强调了导致维格纳矩阵的小群变换序列的几何内容，并将其与球三角学中的经典定理联系起来。


### Abstract

This note summarizes the physics and mathematics of Lorentz transformations for massless particles, specifically for photons. We provide a complete analytical derivation of Wigner's little group matrix and a closed formula for the calculation of Wigner's angle for arbitrary Lorentz transformations. Our derivation highlights the geometrical content of the sequence of little group transformations leading to Wigner's matrix and links it to classical theorems in spherical trigonometry.

## 几何Fano--基于纯化的距离和量子通道分析的Procrustes框架

**Original Title:** A geometric Fano--Procrustes framework for purification-based distances and quantum channels analysis

**Authors:** Tristán M. Osán

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18485v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18485v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

在这项工作中，我们重新制定了乌尔曼纯化重叠优化，并开发了一个基于纯化的几何框架，用于分析混合量子位状态和量子位通道。使用两量子位纯状态的Fano表示，用系统的布洛赫载体、ancilla布洛赫载体和实相关矩阵来描述净化。对于固定的一量子比特混合状态，净化选择的自由度可以通过作用于辅助自由度的适当旋转来参数化。因此，对纯化的优化进入了参考文献中引入的指标\（D_N\）的定义cite{Lamberti 2009}被简化为李群上的一个正交Procrustes问题\（SO（3）\）。这种减少不仅产生了最大的净化重叠，而且产生了与净化框架相关的最佳旋转。从这个旋转中，我们定义了净化失准角\（β\），它提供了基于纯量均匀度的可互换性测量中不包含的几何信息。   该形式主义应用于代表性的量子位通道，包括去极化、位翻转、相翻转、幅度衰减通道和不完美的量子非门。对于保持布洛赫方向的自适应进化，最佳旋转是微不足道的且\（=0\），而非共线的通道动作会产生非零失准。因此，对\（（D_N，eta）\）将最大纯化重叠的幅度与最佳纯化框架的几何重新取向分开。由于最佳的普罗克鲁斯特旋转可以提升为作用于副轴的局部单位，因此该结构还根据副轴侧转换提供了最佳净化的操作解释。


### Abstract

In this work we reformulate the Uhlmann purification-overlap optimization and develop a purification-based geometric framework for the analysis of mixed qubit states and qubit channels. Using the Fano representation of two-qubit pure states, a purification is described in terms of the Bloch vector of the system, the ancilla Bloch vector, and a real correlation matrix. For a fixed one-qubit mixed state, the freedom in the choice of purification can be parametrized by proper rotations acting on the ancillary degrees of freedom. As a result, the optimization over purifications entering the definition of the metric \(D_N\) introduced in Ref.~\cite{Lamberti2009} is reduced to an orthogonal Procrustes problem on the Lie group \(SO(3)\). This reduction yields not only the maximal purification overlap, but also the optimal rotation relating the purification frames. From this rotation we define a purification misalignment angle \(Θ\), which provides geometric information not contained in scalar fidelity-based distinguishability measures.
  The formalism is applied to representative qubit channels, including depolarizing, bit-flip, phase-flip, amplitude-damping channels, and an imperfect quantum NOT gate. For symmetry-adapted evolutions preserving the Bloch-vector direction, the optimal rotation is trivial and \(Θ=0\), whereas noncollinear channel actions generate a nonzero misalignment. The pair \((D_N,Θ)\) therefore separates the magnitude of the maximal purification overlap from the geometric reorientation of the optimal purification frames. Since the optimal Procrustes rotation can be lifted to a local unitary acting on the ancilla, the construction also provides an operational interpretation of the optimal purification in terms of an ancilla-side transformation.


---


## 强相关费米子的量子魔力$-$哈伯德二聚体

**Original Title:** Quantum magic of strongly correlated fermions $-$ the Hubbard dimer

**Authors:** Edoardo Zavatti, Gabriele Bellomia, Massimo Capone

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18494v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18494v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们研究了哈伯德二聚体的非稳定性（量子魔法）含量，哈伯德二聚体是一种分析可解但完全非平凡的强相关费米子模型。我们可以访问零温度和有限温度特性以及量子猝灭协议中的时间演变。我们使用魔法的鲁棒性和稳定器雷尼（Renyi）熵来评估局部和非局部非稳定性，证明后者如何经常无法检测到通常在此类系统中发现的混合稳定器状态。最后，我们将非稳定性与量子状态复杂性的其他真正资源进行比较，即，费米子非高斯性和超选择两点纠缠。我们的发现证实了非稳定性作为一种根本不同的量子资源的概念，能够提供更传统的信息论量所忽视的深刻见解。


### Abstract

We study the non-stabilizerness (quantum magic) content of the Hubbard dimer, an analytically solvable, yet completely non-trivial, model of strongly correlated fermions. We can access zero- and finite-temperature properties as well as the time evolution in a quantum quench protocol. We evaluate local and nonlocal non-stabilizerness using both the robustness of magic and the stabilizer Renyi entropy, demonstrating how the latter often fails in detecting the mixed stabilizer states that are typically found in this kind of systems. Finally, we compare the non-stabilizerness with other genuine resources of quantum-state complexity, i.e., the fermionic non-Gaussianity and the superselected two-site entanglement. Our findings corroborate the notion of non-stabilizerness as a fundamentally different quantum resource, able to give profound insights that are missed by more traditional information-theoretic quantities.


---


## 基于过渡金属二硫属化合物碳缺陷的电信波量子发射器

**Original Title:** Quantum Emitters at Telecommunication Wavelengths based on Carbon Defects in Transition Metal Dichalcogenides

**Authors:** Chanaprom Cholsuk, Sujin Suwanna, Tobias Vogl

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18501v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18501v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

低维材料已成为量子发射体的有前途的宿主，其发射通常源于应变诱导的能带弯曲或缺陷诱导的两级系统。在这些材料中，过渡金属二硫属化合物（TJ）单层引起了特别的关注;然而，它们的性能受到室温下强光致发光（PL）猝灭的限制。当从单层转变为多层时，随着MTD从直接带隙转变为间接带隙，我们在本文中提出了一种通过利用MTD双层的间接带隙结合点缺陷掺杂来克服这种猝灭限制的策略。间接间隙抑制激子PL，而特定缺陷则实现稳健的缺陷介导量子发射。利用混合函密度函式理论，我们研究了WS 2、WSe 2、MoS 2和MoSe 2双层中硫族位（S和Se）上的取代碳缺陷，并全面描述了它们的光学性质。中性和单负电荷状态都被发现是热力学稳定的。中性缺陷在O和C频段电信窗口中表现出具有发射的单重态配置，而带负电的缺陷则采用具有旋转选择性转变和近红外发射的双重态配置。发现电子-音素耦合强度、辐射寿命和偶极取向敏感地取决于宿主材料和缺陷部位，为实验识别提供了不同的指纹。因此，我们的研究结果确立了碳掺杂的MTD双层作为在电信波长下工作的室温缺陷量子发射器的有前途的平台。


### Abstract

Low-dimensional materials have emerged as promising hosts for quantum emitters, whose emission typically arises from either strain-induced band bending or defect-induced two-level systems. Among these materials, transition metal dichalcogenide (TMD) monolayers have attracted particular attention; however, their performance is limited by strong photoluminescence (PL) quenching at room temperature. As TMDs transition from a direct to an indirect bandgap when moving from monolayers to multilayers, we herein propose a strategy to overcome this quenching limitation by exploiting the indirect bandgap of TMD bilayers in combination with a point defect doping. The indirect gap suppresses excitonic PL, while specific defects enable robust defect-mediated quantum emission. Using hybrid-functional density functional theory, we investigate substitutional carbon defects at chalcogen sites (S and Se) in WS2, WSe2, MoS2, and MoSe2 bilayers and comprehensively characterize their optical properties. Both neutral and singly negative charge states are found to be thermodynamically stable. Neutral defects exhibit singlet configurations with emission in the O- and C-band telecommunication windows, whereas negatively charged defects adopt doublet configurations featuring spin-selective transitions and near-infrared emission. The electron-phonon coupling strength, radiative lifetime, and dipole orientation are found to depend sensitively on both the host material and defect site, providing distinct fingerprints for experimental identification. Our findings, therefore, establish carbon-doped TMD bilayers as promising platforms for room-temperature defect-based quantum emitters operating at telecommunication wavelengths.


---


## 光路多体量子光学的实现

**Original Title:** Realization of waveguide many-body quantum optics

**Authors:** Lena M. Hansen, Clara Henke, Christoph Hotter, Oliver A. D. Sandberg, Thomas Wilkens Sandø, Vasiliki Angelopoulou, Alexey Tiranov, Christoffer B. Møller, Zhe Liu, Leonardo Midolo, Nikolai Bart, Arne Ludwig, Philip Walther, Cornelis J. van Diepen, Peter Lodahl, Anders Søndberg Sørensen

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18525v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18525v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

逐个量子控制光是量子光学的核心。在基本层面上，量子相互作用是通过与原子的耦合来调节的，最终控制需要单量子与单原子的确定性光物质界面。将这一范式扩展到以确定性和可扩展的方式辐射耦合多个单个原子，打开了多体量子光学的领域。在这里，我们通过将固体人造原子与纳米光电子导体相干耦合来实现这样的设置，并展示由量子发射体数量控制的更高级的量子相关性。我们研究了由发射极-光散射引起的非线性光输运的标度，并证明添加量子发射极会产生更高级的光相关性。具体来说，我们通过实验观察到一对集体耦合的发射体的真正三量子相关性，而较低的量子数的贡献被抑制。此外，我们还扩展到三个耦合到导管的共振量子发射器。这些进步证明了多体量子光学在多体量子电动力学中的出现，从而实现了新的量子量子模拟器、多体纠缠态的创建以及新型量子相转变的探索。


### Abstract

Controlling light photon-by-photon is central to quantum optics. At a fundamental level, photon interactions are mediated by their coupling to atoms, and ultimate control requires deterministic light-matter interfacing of single photons to single atoms. Extending this paradigm to radiatively couple multiple individual atoms in a deterministic and scalable manner opens the arena of many-body quantum optics. Here, we realize such a setting by coherently coupling solid-state artificial atoms to a nanophotonic waveguide and demonstrate higher-order photon correlations that are controlled by the number of quantum emitters. We study the scaling of nonlinear photonic transport induced by emitter-photon scattering and demonstrate that adding a quantum emitter generates higher-order photon correlations. Specifically, we experimentally observe genuine three-photon correlations from a pair of collectively coupled emitters, while contributions from lower photon numbers are suppressed. In addition, we scale to three resonant quantum emitters coupled to the waveguide. These advancements demonstrate the onset of many-body quantum optics in waveguide quantum electrodynamics, enabling new photonic quantum simulators, the creation of many-body entangled states, and the exploration of novel quantum phase transitions.


---


## CLARST决策树：通过基于数据的建议实现自动化

**Original Title:** The QuaST Decision Tree: Achieving Automation With Data-Based Recommendations

**Authors:** Benedikt Poggel, Lena Tokuhiro, Georg Kruse, Jeanette Miriam Lorenz

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18539v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18539v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

量子计算机越来越强大。用于开发量子增强算法的软件工具正在成熟。然而，软件栈仍然缺乏与应用程序的连接，无法实现结合经典和量子计算步骤的混合算法。最终用户需要得到帮助来选择预处理、后处理、经典和量子算法选项的最佳组合。因此，面向应用程序的软件栈需要涵盖问题建模、编码、算法选择和超参数调优。有多种工具可用于具体建议。CLARST决策树反映了在其模块化网络结构中组合单个决策的复杂性，该结构由灵活的计算节点和模块化建议组成。它可以轻松配置为在工业求解器、高性能计算软件栈中服务，或用于开发中的快速原型设计。自动化的关键要素是通过模块交付。我们提出了一个这样的模块，用于根据稳健的可扩展性分析和问题实例的分类来判断变分算法的可行性。自动化提高了端到端解决方案的性能，凸显了混合量子解决方案的好处，减少了昂贵的试错测试，并提高了量子设备的利用率，以获得实际利益。


### Abstract

Quantum computers are increasingly powerful. Software tools for the development of quantum-enhanced algorithms are maturing. However, the software stack still lacks the connection to applications that would enable hybrid algorithms combining classical and quantum computing steps. End users need to be assisted in choosing the best combination of preprocessing, postprocessing, classical and quantum algorithms options. The application-facing software stack is therefore required to cover problem modeling, encoding, algorithm selection and hyperparameter tuning. A variety of tools exist for specific recommendations. The QuaST Decision Tree reflects the complexity in combining individual decisions in its modular network structure, consisting of flexible computation nodes with modular recommendations. It can easily be configured to serve in an industrial solver, an HPC software stack, or for rapid prototyping in development. The key ingredient, automation, is delivered by modules. We present one such module judging the feasibility of variational algorithms based on a robust scalability analysis and classification of problem instances. The automation improves the performance of end-to-end solutions, highlights the benefit to be gained from the hybrid quantum solution, reduces expensive trial-and-error testing, and leads to an improved utilization of quantum devices for a practical benefit.


---


## 使用蒙特卡罗树搜索发现量子经典神经网络的数据编码策略

**Original Title:** Discovering Data Encoding Strategies for Quantum-Classical Neural Networks Using Monte Carlo Tree Search

**Authors:** Lena Tokuhiro, Amine Bentellis, Jeanette Miriam Lorenz

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18540v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18540v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

量子机器学习（QML）引起了相当大的研究兴趣，但它是否比经典方法提供实际好处仍然是一个悬而未决的问题。数据编码的选择显着影响QML性能，但为什么某些编码优于其他编码仍然知之甚少。我们采用蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）来发现量子经典卷积神经网络（QCCNN）的最佳数据编码电路，该网络将用于特征提取的非变分量子块与经典分类器相结合。在评估两个医学成像数据集时，发现的电路优于常用的编码策略，同时与纯粹的经典电路相比显示出有竞争力的结果。我们进一步分析指标，以确定预测编码性能。纠缠能力和傅立叶分解提供了最小的洞察力，而特征图的有效秩表现出有意义的相关性，可以作为阈值标准来加速搜索高性能编码。我们的研究结果提供了一个实用的方法，编码发现和新的见解是什么使数据编码有效的QML。


### Abstract

Quantum machine learning (QML) has attracted considerable research interest, yet whether it offers practical benefits over classical approaches remains an open question. The choice of data encoding significantly influences QML performance, but why certain encodings outperform others remains poorly understood. We employ Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) to discover optimal data encoding circuits for a quantum-classical convolutional neural network (QCCNN) combining a non-variational quantum block for feature extraction with a classical classifier. Evaluating on two medical imaging datasets, the discovered circuits outperform commonly used encoding strategies while showing competitive results compared to purely classical counterparts. We further analyze metrics to identify predictors of encoding performance. Entanglement capability and Fourier decomposition provide minimal insight, whereas the effective rank of the feature maps exhibits meaningful correlation and can serve as a threshold criterion to accelerate the search for high-performing encodings. Our findings provide both a practical method for encoding discovery and new insights into what makes data encodings effective in QML.

## 纯量$-$张量引力作为广义黑洞熵的探索

**Original Title:** Scalar$-$Tensor Gravity as a Probe of Generalized Black Hole Entropy

**Authors:** Hussain Gohar

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18551v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18551v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们通过建立与引力的纯量$-$张量理论中Misner$-$Sharp准局部质量和Wald Noether$-$荷质的直接对应关系，发展了一类广泛的广义黑洞熵函的几何实现。由此产生的模型具有与尺度相关的有效引力耦合，其功能依赖性由基础的熵参数决定。在这个框架内，我们推导出了显式的爱因斯坦框架纯量势：对于巴罗（Barrow）来说，是一个陡峭的指数势;对于Tsallis$-$Cirto（Tsallis）来说，是一个由非扩张性参数决定的指数势;对于量子引力和纠缠$-$诱导的修正，是一个大约线性的势。这些不同的势产生了特征性的宇宙现象学，对暴胀动力学、后期暗能量行为和非奇异弹跳宇宙学产生了影响。该框架与当前太阳系测试、大爆炸核合成和脉冲星定时观测的约束是兼容的，它产生的预测可以通过即将到来的观测调查来探测。这样，分析建立了一个统一的和几何接地之间的联系信息$-$理论熵的建议和引力场理论。


### Abstract

We develop a geometric realization of a broad class of generalized black hole entropy functionals by establishing their direct correspondence with the Misner$-$Sharp quasilocal mass and the Wald Noether$-$charge entropy in scalar$-$tensor theories of gravity. The resulting models feature a scale-dependent effective gravitational coupling, whose functional dependence is determined by the underlying entropy parameters. Within this framework, we derive explicit Einstein-frame scalar potentials: for Barrow entropy, a steep exponential potential; for Tsallis$-$Cirto entropy, an exponential potential governed by the nonextensivity parameter; and for quantum-gravity and entanglement$-$induced corrections, an approximately linear potential. These distinct potentials generate characteristic cosmological phenomenology, with implications for inflationary dynamics, late-time dark-energy behavior, and non-singular bouncing cosmologies. The framework is compatible with current constraints from solar-system tests, big-bang nucleosynthesis, and pulsar-timing observations, and it yields predictions that can be probed by forthcoming observational surveys. In this way, the analysis establishes a unified and geometrically grounded connection between information$-$theoretic entropy proposals and gravitational field theory.


---


## 强化学习辅助多体兴奋状态和实时动力学的量子模拟

**Original Title:** Reinforcement Learning Assisted Quantum Simulation of Many-Body Excited States and Real-Time Dynamics

**Authors:** Jiaji Zhang, Lipeng Chen, Carlos L. Benavides-Riveros

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18569v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18569v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

多费米子系统的电子激发态和实时量子动力学的计算是近期量子计算最有前途的应用之一。在这项工作中，我们将之前为底态问题开发的强化学习契约量子本征解算器（RL-CQE）推广到电子激发态和实时量子动力学，其中深度Q网络代理在每次迭代时自适应地选择二体操作符，产生更紧凑的反式和更好的鲁棒性。关键超参数。该算法的一个关键特征是基于ACSE剩余的可扩展状态表示，其维度随着单粒子基础而增长，但保持独立于目标激发状态的数量。我们还验证了激励状态环境中无符号量子位运算符的等效性，扩展了之前为底态问题建立的结果。我们的时间演化RL-CQE源自一个恒标度类比，它代表具有固定数量的么正变换的波函数，独立于模拟时间$t$，由激发态的净化系综处理的共享么正结构实现。化学系统的基准证明了化学准确性，在一系列键长内操作员计数最少。


### Abstract

The computation of electronic excited states and real-time quantum dynamics of many-fermion systems is among the most promising applications of near-term quantum computing. In this work, we generalize the reinforcement learning contracted quantum eigensolver (RL-CQE), previously developed for ground-state problems, to electronic excited states and real-time quantum dynamics, in which a deep Q-network agent adaptively selects the two-body operators at each iteration, yielding more compact ansätze and improved robustness with respect to critical hyperparameters. A key feature of the algorithm is a scalable state representation based on the ACSE residuals, whose dimension grows with the one-particle basis but remains independent of the number of targeted excited states. We also verify the equivalence of sign-free qubit operators in the excited-state setting, extending a result previously established for ground-state problems. Our RL-CQE for time evolution derives from a constant-scaling ansatz that represents the wave function with a fixed number of unitary transformations independent of simulation time $t$, enabled by the shared unitary structure of the purified ensemble treatment of excited states. Benchmarks on chemical systems demonstrate chemical accuracy with minimal operator counts across a range of bond lengths.


---


## 双带汉密尔顿学派的Krylov复杂性和保真度敏感性

**Original Title:** Krylov complexity and fidelity susceptibility in two-band Hamiltonians

**Authors:** Rishav Chaudhuri, Ayush Raj, Soham Ray, Sai Satyam Samal

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18594v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18594v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们研究了两带汉密尔顿体的基状态的Krylov传播复杂性，其中参考状态是布洛赫球上的一般状态。传播复杂度是通过使用布洛赫球数据的纯几何公式来获得的，而无需构造电路Hamilton。对于一般参考状态，在Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）模型中的拓广复杂度的求导在拓广阶段存在显着差异。我们证明，对于一般两带模型，传播复杂性的求导受到保真度敏感性的限制，这表明传播复杂性对任何间隙闭合（拓扑或平凡）的敏感性。这一点在具有微小间隙闭合的巨大狄拉克Hamilton量中得到了说明。最后，我们在SSH模型中的布局阶段和平凡阶段之间引入了非正二元性，这体现在传播复杂性和保真度敏感性上。


### Abstract

We investigate Krylov spread complexity for the ground state of two-band Hamiltonians, where the reference state is a generic state on the Bloch sphere. The spread complexity is obtained by using a purely geometric formulation in terms of Bloch sphere data without constructing the circuit Hamiltonian. For generic reference states, the derivative of the spread complexity is logarithmically divergent at the topological phase transition in the Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) model. We demonstrate that the derivative of the spread complexity is bounded by fidelity susceptibility for general two-band models, indicating the sensitivity of the spread complexity to any gap closing (topological or trivial). This is illustrated in the massive Dirac Hamiltonian with a trivial gap closing. Finally, we introduce a non-unitary duality in the SSH model between the topological and trivial phases, which manifests itself in the spread complexity and fidelity susceptibility.


---


## 基于施密特数的非高斯纠缠层次

**Original Title:** Non-Gaussian Entanglement Hierarchy Based on the Schmidt Number

**Authors:** Jiajie Guo, Shuheng Liu, Matteo Fadel, Qiongyi He

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18605v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18605v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

非高斯纠缠是各种量子任务中一种有前途的资源。最近定义的类识别了无法通过对可分离输入应用高斯运算来生成的纠缠。为了进一步探索这种上下文中的纠缠，我们在二元玻色子系统中引入了一个定量见证$E_{\rm NG}$，对于所有高斯可纠缠状态，它满足$E_{\rm NG}=1$，而$E_{\rm NG}>1$证明非高斯纠缠。它的上限$d=\lceil E_{\rm NG}\rceil$提供了无法通过高斯变换约化的施密特数的下限，从而定义了非高斯纠缠的自然层次结构。对于纯状态来说，条件是尖锐的，并且分层反映了状态学习的复杂性。我们用一些典型的非高斯状态（例如NOON状态和压缩Kerr状态）对框架进行基准测试，并分析其对损失的鲁棒性。此外，我们构建了一个实验上经济的NOON型证人，仅需要四个投影测量，其中推导出分析高斯纠缠阈值。这些结果建立了一个具有操作意义且在实验上可访问的框架，用于识别连续变量量子平台中的非高斯纠缠资源。


### Abstract

Non-Gaussian entanglement is a promising resource in various quantum tasks. A recently defined class identifies entanglement that cannot be generated by applying Gaussian operations to separable inputs. To further explore the entanglement in this context, we introduce a quantitative witness $E_{\rm NG}$ in bipartite bosonic systems, which satisfies $E_{\rm NG}=1$ for all Gaussian-entanglable states, while $E_{\rm NG}>1$ certifies non-Gaussian entanglement. Its ceiling $d=\lceil E_{\rm NG}\rceil$ provides a lower bound on the Schmidt number irreducible by Gaussian transformations, thereby defining a natural hierarchy of non-Gaussian entanglement. For pure states, the condition is sharp and the hierarchy reflects the complexity of state learning. We benchmark the framework with some paradigmatic non-Gaussian states, such as NOON states and squeezed Kerr states, and analyze its robustness against loss. Moreover, we construct an experimentally economical NOON-type witness requiring only four projective measurements, where an analytical Gaussian-entanglable threshold is derived. These results establish an operationally meaningful and experimentally accessible framework for identifying non-Gaussian entanglement resources in continuous-variable quantum platforms.


---


## 装饰的Rule-54量子元胞自动机上的斐波那契多体伤疤

**Original Title:** Fibonacci many-body scars in a decorated Rule-54 quantum cellular automaton

**Authors:** Han-Ze Li, Jian-Xin Zhong

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18622v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18622v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

量子多体伤痕提供了一种受控形式的弱历经破缺，其中结构化的非热本征态与热化多体光谱共存。我们基于Rule-54量子元胞自动机的固有孤立子结构，引入了一种量子比特级路径来精确疤痕。规则54的硬核二聚体部分提供了一个完全可翻译的受保护骨架，而局部投影仪控制的装饰在该骨架上是不可见的，在其外部也是不平凡的。因此，受保护的动力学可以简化为有限的翻译轨道，其傅里叶模式形成具有亚体积定律纠缠的精确Floquet本征状态。精确伤疤的数量随着斐波那契组合而增加，而它们在完整量子位希尔伯特空间中的比例仍然呈指数级小。粒子大小模拟显示了装饰补中的页面状本征态纠缠、快速纠缠增长、保真度衰变和圆形正系综准能量统计。这种结构表明，可以从相互作用的可逆自动机的原生有限轨道结构中设计出精确的多体伤痕，并为伤痕细胞自动机动力学的数字量子模拟提供了直接的起点。


### Abstract

Quantum many-body scars provide a controlled form of weak ergodicity breaking, in which structured nonthermal eigenstates coexist with a thermalizing many-body spectrum. We introduce a qubit-level route to exact scars based on the intrinsic soliton structure of the Rule-54 quantum cellular automaton. A hard-core dimer sector of Rule 54 supplies an exactly translatable protected skeleton, while local projector-controlled decorations are invisible on this skeleton and nontrivial outside it. The protected dynamics is therefore reducible to finite translation orbits, whose Fourier modes form exact Floquet eigenstates with sub-volume-law entanglement. The number of exact scars grows with Fibonacci combinatorics, whereas their fraction in the full qubit Hilbert space remains exponentially small. Finite-size simulations show Page-like eigenstate entanglement, rapid entanglement growth, fidelity decay, and circular unitary ensemble quasienergy statistics in the decorated complement. This construction demonstrates that exact many-body scars can be engineered from native finite-orbit structures of an interacting reversible automaton, and provides a direct starting point for digital quantum simulation of scarred cellular-automaton dynamics.

## 没有完全积极性的开放量子动力学：批评

**Original Title:** Open quantum dynamics without Complete Positivity: a criticism

**Authors:** Fabio Benatti, Dariusz Chruściński, Saverio Pascazio

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18639v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18639v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

完全正性的要求经常被视为描述开放量子动力学的基本一致性条件。我们批判性地审查这一要求，并讨论其物理动机和局限性。我们分析基于将非完全正映射的域限制为兼容初始状态子集的提案。以各向同性状态为具体例子，我们表明，随着系统维度的增长，此类领域限制变得越来越严重，揭示了基于相容性的方法的内在弱点。


### Abstract

The requirement of complete positivity is very often regarded as a fundamental consistency condition for the description of open quantum dynamics. We critically examine this requirement and discuss both its physical motivations and its limitations. We analyze proposals based on restricting the domain of non-completely positive maps to subsets of compatible initial states. Using isotropic states as a concrete example, we show that such domain restrictions become increasingly severe with growing system dimension, revealing an intrinsic weakness of the compatibility-based approach.

## Reeh-Schlieder状态准备的模块下界

**Original Title:** Modular Lower Bounds on Reeh-Schlieder State Preparation

**Authors:** Javier Blanco-Romero, Florina Almenares Mendoza

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18640v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18640v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

Reeh-Schlieder定理认为，每个目标载体都可以通过局部化在任意小时空区域中的操作员从真空中逼近，但它不会给出这样做的量化成本。本注释将标准Tomita-Takesaki估计隔离为与模型无关的准备界限。模块化能源严重负能量的目标需要大型本地运营商。将这样的操作员重新缩放到物理收缩后，相同的估计成为选择后费用的下限。在模汉密尔顿量已知的几何中，界限变得明确。Bisognano-Wichmann将其转化为楔形的助推能量陈述，而Casini-Huerta-Myers公式则为共形场论的有界区域提供了一个应力张量版本。局部正只能达到非负模能状态。负模部门需要非正或后选择的结果，从而给出了一个准备成本界限，以补充III型局部代数中的真空挪用。


### Abstract

The Reeh-Schlieder theorem says that every target vector can be approximated from the vacuum by an operator localized in an arbitrarily small spacetime region, but it gives no quantitative cost for doing so. This note isolates a standard Tomita-Takesaki estimate as a model-independent preparation bound. Targets with deeply negative modular energy require large local operators. After rescaling such an operator to a physical contraction, the same estimate becomes a lower bound on postselection overhead. In geometries where the modular Hamiltonian is known, the bound becomes explicit. Bisognano-Wichmann turns it into a boost energy statement for wedges, and the Casini-Huerta-Myers formula gives a stress-tensor version for bounded regions of conformal field theories. Local unitaries can only reach states of nonnegative modular energy. Negative modular sectors require nonunitary or postselected outcomes, giving a preparation cost bound that complements vacuum embezzlement in type III local algebras.


---


## 振荡器的通用Jaynes-Cummings控制

**Original Title:** Universal Jaynes-Cummings Control of an Oscillator

**Authors:** Jordan Huang, Ethan Kasaba, Thomas J. DiNapoli, Tanay Roy, Srivatsan Chakram

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18658v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18658v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

杰尼斯-卡明斯（JC）相互作用--二水平系统和谐振子之间激发的相干交换--是量子光学的基本相互作用之一，跨腔量子电动力学、俘获离子、机械共振器和超导体电路等平台实现。尽管JC相互作用和量子位旋转形成了用于振荡器控制的通用门集，但实际实现尚未得到演示。在这里，我们通过将任意一元门编译成JC相互作用和量子位旋转的序列来开发并实验演示通用的基于JC的振荡器控制。在我们的实验中，使用高品质因子微波腔的模式和使用超传输子电路的辅助量子位来实现振荡器，JC相互作用通过约瑟夫森非线性实现的边带相互作用来实现。原生门被构建为在所选截止量子数以下关闭，编码具有抑制的泄漏误差的qudit，而辅助松弛误差是可检测的。我们进一步发现，频散漂移可以作为减少电路深度的编译资源。我们演示了通用qudit控制，并实现了平均选后工艺保真度为96%的单quotri门集，以及quotri和quququint转移门。这些结果将Jaynes-Cummings控制确立为通用振荡器控制的实用途径，使可编程玻色子处理器能够跨各种量子平台。


### Abstract

The Jaynes-Cummings (JC) interaction-the coherent exchange of excitations between a two-level system and a harmonic oscillator-is one of the fundamental interactions of quantum optics, realized across platforms such as cavity quantum electrodynamics, trapped ions, mechanical resonators, and superconducting circuits. Although JC interactions and qubit rotations form a universal gate set for oscillator control, practical implementations have not been demonstrated. Here we develop and experimentally demonstrate universal JC-based oscillator control by compiling arbitrary unitary gates into sequences of JC interactions and qubit rotations. In our experiment, the oscillator is realized using a mode of a high quality factor microwave cavity and the ancilla qubit using a superconducting transmon circuit, with the JC interaction implemented by a sideband interaction enabled by the Josephson nonlinearity. The native gates are constructed to be closed below a chosen cutoff photon number, encoding a qudit with suppressed leakage errors, while ancilla relaxation errors are detectable. We further find that the dispersive shift serves as a compilation resource that reduces circuit depths. We demonstrate universal qudit control and implement a single-qutrit gate set with a mean post-selected process fidelity of 96%, as well as ququart and ququint shift gates. These results establish Jaynes-Cummings control as a practical route to universal oscillator control, enabling programmable bosonic processors across a variety of quantum platforms.


---


## 非对称星型网络中量子会议密钥协商策略优化

**Original Title:** Strategy optimization for quantum conference key agreement in asymmetric star networks

**Authors:** Janka Memmen, Julia Kunzelmann, Nathan Walk, Jens Eisert, Julius Wallnöfer

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18677v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18677v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

纠缠态的分布是促进量子通信的量子网络的核心任务，并且多体纠缠态的使用具有其自身的一系列考虑。在这项工作中，我们分析了一个量子会议协议的基础上GHZ态的网络中的一个中心站，多个客户端连接。使用全面的数值模拟，我们研究如何微小的变化，如当事人的数量，内存的数量，从中央站的不对称距离，可以极大地影响协议的性能。特别是，我们证明了通过优化截止时间来调整策略是至关重要的。从更广泛的角度来看，我们认为，数值模拟是一个不可或缺的工具，为量子通信设计现实的方案的协议设计。


### Abstract

The distribution of entangled states is a core task for quantum networks facilitating quantum communication, and the use of multipartite entangled states comes with its own set of considerations. In this work, we analyze a quantum conference agreement protocol based on GHZ states in a network with a central station to which multiple clients are connected. Using comprehensive numerical simulations, we investigate how minor variations in the scenario-such as the number of parties, the number of memories, and asymmetric distances from the central station-can drastically influence the performance of the protocol. In particular, we demonstrate that it is crucial to adjust the strategy by optimizing cutoff times. From a broader perspective, we argue that numerical simulations are an indispensable tool for protocol design for devising realistic schemes for quantum communication.

## 量子气实验的机器学习可以解释吗？

**Original Title:** Can machine learning for quantum-gas experiments be explainable?

**Authors:** I. B. Spielman amd J. P. Zwolak

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18689v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18689v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

多体原子物理学的几乎所有方面都具有挑战性：实验在技术上要求很高，数据集变得巨大，并且通用量子系统的经典模拟的存储器和中央处理器需求通常随着系统大小而呈指数级增长。机器学习（ML）方法已经在这些领域提供了帮助，并且有望带来变革。在这里，我们重点关注ML在基于冷原子的量子模拟器中的两个具体应用。这些设备通常以图像的形式生成数据;我们首先展示原始图像的去噪，然后识别玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中的孤波。在这两个例子中，我们都会评论性能、模型复杂性和可解释性之间的相互作用。


### Abstract

Virtually all aspects of many-body atomic physics are challenging: experiments are technically demanding, datasets have become enormous, and the memory and CPU requirements for classical simulation of generic quantum systems often scale exponentially with system size. Machine learning (ML) methods are already assisting in each of these areas and are poised to become transformative. Here, we focus on two specific applications of ML to cold-atom-based quantum simulators. These devices generally generate data in the form of images; we first showcase denoising of raw images and then identify solitonic waves in Bose-Einstein condensates. In both of these examples, we comment on the interplay between performance, model complexity, and interpretability.

## 检测压缩状态随机位移副本中的非经典性

**Original Title:** Detecting nonclassicality in randomly-displaced copies of a squeezed state

**Authors:** Mehmet Emre Tasgin

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18708v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18708v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们解决了一个基本问题：当每个副本以不同的位移/幅度到达时，人们能否确定接收到的信号是否被压缩？我们引入了一个相互作用Hamilton，它将象限压缩转化为数字压缩。使用此转换，我们测试副本是否满足$g^{（2）}（0）<1$。汉密尔顿量本身并不创造非经典性;它只是将其从四次压缩转移到数字压缩。这使我们能够识别挤压，即使当单个副本具有随机位移。


### Abstract

We address a fundamental question: Can one determine whether a received signal is squeezed when each copy arrives with a different displacement/amplitude? We introduce an interaction Hamiltonian that converts quadrature squeezing into number squeezing. Using this conversion, we test whether the copies satisfy $g^{(2)}(0)<1$. The Hamiltonian itself does not create nonclassicality; it only transfers it from quadrature squeezing to number squeezing. This allows us to identify squeezing even when individual copies have random displacements.

## 量子香农理论变得强大：几乎独立的三种协议的故事来源

**Original Title:** Quantum Shannon theory made robust: a tale of three protocols for almost i.i.d. sources

**Authors:** Filippo Girardi, Nilanjana Datta, Giacomo De Palma, Ludovico Lami

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18726v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18726v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

信息论协议的渐进率（包括误差指数、压缩率和通道容量）传统上是在理想化的假设下定义的，即基础资源（状态或通道）是独立且同分布的（i.i.d.）。有些令人惊讶的是，即使与确切的i. i. d略有偏差。结构可能会导致这些协议的严重崩溃。信息论协议的渐进率--误差指数、压缩率、容量--最初的评估是理所当然地认为底层源（状态或通道）是i. i. d。与我们乍一看可能的预期不同，不难展示当i.i. d时可能会严重失败的协议实例。假设仅大致成立，而不是完全成立。如果i. i. d扰动的确切性质如果政权是已知的（例如逐点缺陷），我们可以设计一个定制协议来补偿缺陷（例如，通过丢弃损坏的子系统）。然而，在任何现实环境中，i.i. d也不能。系统的行为得到精确保证，也无法准确确定与理想制度的偏差。在本文中，我们回答了以下问题：当i.i.d.资源被任何任意的几乎i. i. d所取代。沿着它的资源？未知扰动的性质是什么，在哪些情况下，此类协议是可能的？我们特别关注假设测试、数据压缩和通道编码。作为我们分析的副产品，我们引入了球杆距离的概念，作为众所周知的钻石距离的变体，也是几乎独立的。过程，这可能具有独立兴趣。


### Abstract

The asymptotic rates of information-theoretic protocols - including error exponents, compression rates, and channel capacities - are traditionally defined under the idealised assumption that the underlying resource (state or channel) is independent and identically distributed (i.i.d.). Somewhat surprisingly, even slight departures from the exact i.i.d. structure can lead to a drastic breakdown of these protocols. The asymptotic rates of information theoretic protocols - error exponents, compression rates, capacities - were originally evaluated taking for granted that the underlying source (state or channel) is i.i.d. Differently from what we might expect at first glance, it is not hard to exhibit instances of protocols that may drastically fail when the i.i.d. assumption holds only approximately rather than exactly. If the precise nature of the perturbation from the i.i.d. regime is known (e.g. a pointwise defect), we could design a bespoke protocol that compensates for the defect (for example, by discarding the corrupted subsystem). However, in any realistic setting, neither can the i.i.d. behaviour of the system be precisely guaranteed, nor can the deviations from the ideal regime be determined exactly. In this paper we answer the following question: are there protocols that can still achieve the optimal asymptotic rates when the i.i.d. resource is replaced by any arbitrary almost i.i.d. resource along it? What is the nature of the unknown perturbation under which protocols like these are possible? We focus, in particular, on hypothesis testing, data compression, and channel coding. As a by-product of our analysis, we introduce the notion of club distance, as a variant of the well-known diamond distance, and of an almost i.i.d. process, which may be of independent interest.


---


## 通过空间相关非平衡噪音检测漩涡运动

**Original Title:** Detecting vortex motion through spatially correlated nonequilibrium noise

**Authors:** Yifan F. Zhang, Rhine Samajdar, Sarang Gopalakrishnan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18941v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18941v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

接近超临界相的阻输运可能源于正常状态准粒子或涡旋的运动。仅靠导电性并不能区分这些机制。我们提出了一种明确的方法来区分它们，使用最近开发的协方差磁力测量实验工具，该工具使用钻石中的氮空位中心来探测磁噪音中的实时时空相关性。我们的关键见解是，在外加电流下，底层电荷子在样本上方的空间相关磁噪音中留下方向指纹：普通电子平行于电流漂移，而涡旋由于马格努斯力，垂直于电流漂移。噪音协方差检测这种各向异性并识别涡旋驱动的运输性质。我们计算了代表性薄膜超导体的预期噪音相关性，并证明各向异性信号完全在当前实验能力的范围内。


### Abstract

Resistive transport near a superconducting phase can arise from the motion of normal-state quasiparticles or that of vortices. The conductivity alone does not distinguish between these mechanisms. We propose an unambiguous method for telling them apart, using the recently developed experimental tool of covariance magnetometry, which uses nitrogen-vacancy centers in diamond to probe real-time spatiotemporal correlations in magnetic noise. Our key insight is that, under an applied current, the underlying charge carriers leave a directional fingerprint in the spatially correlated magnetic noise above the sample: ordinary electric carriers drift parallel to the current, whereas vortices, owing to the Magnus force, drift perpendicular to it. The noise covariance detects this anisotropy and identifies the vortex-driven nature of transport. We compute the noise correlations expected for a representative thin-film superconductor and demonstrate that the anisotropic signal is well within the reach of current experimental capabilities.

## 量子场论中两点函数的非微扰测量

**Original Title:** Non-perturbative measurements of two-point functions in quantum field theory

**Authors:** Sebastian Holmén, T. Rick Perche

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18945v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18945v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们提出了一种非微扰方法，通过该方法，局部探测器可以访问时空区域内量子场的两点函数。通过考虑无间隙粒子探测器网格，我们识别了编码场两点函数的探测可观测量。我们通过对涂抹两点函数进行时空多极展开来量化物理有限大小相互作用区域引入的差异。我们的协议完全按照可测量的检测器相关性来表达两点函数，提供了QFT中状态的操作概念。


### Abstract

We present a non-perturbative method through which local probes can access the two-point function of a quantum field within a region of spacetime. By considering a lattice of gapless particle detectors, we identified the probe observables that encode the field's two-point function. We quantify the discrepancies introduced by physical finite-sized interaction regions by performing a spacetime multipole expansion of the smeared two-point function. Our protocol expresses the two-point function entirely in terms of measurable detectors correlations, providing an operational notion of states in QFT.

## 噪音诱导的可模拟性从操作员加扰的转变

**Original Title:** Noise-induced Simulability Transition from Operator Scrambling

**Authors:** Neil Dowling, Xhek Turkeshi, Jacopo De Nardis, Guglielmo Lami

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18943v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18943v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

在海森堡图像中模拟量子多体动力学或量子计算的复杂性取决于最初简单的操作符扰乱成指数级多的泡利弦的叠加。相应的展开系数定义了泡利谱，其结构控制基于截断泡利展开的经典算法的性能。在这里，我们确定随机量子电路的有限深度泡利谱，无论是在无噪音的情况下还是在存在局部噪音的情况下，都是通过由运营商稳定器雷尼动量给出的。在无噪电路中，我们发现了完全扰乱状态的方法中的一个层次：低矩在相对较短的深度处平衡，而对罕见的大幅度泡利系数敏感的较高矩需要参数化更大的深度。在有噪的电路中，加扰与对运营商传播的有效抑制竞争。超过每个周期的临界误差$γ_c N=\mathCal{O}（1）$，操作符无法达到完全加扰的分布，并且仍然支持泡利字符串的热力稀疏子集。相反，在这个规模以下，我们严格证明经典模拟仍然是指数级困难的，证明有限噪音并不自动意味着经典的可模拟性。因此，由此产生的噪音引发的操作员复杂性转变划定了本质上硬的量子动力学和经典可访问的量子动力学之间的边界。


### Abstract

The complexity of simulating quantum many-body dynamics, or quantum computations, in the Heisenberg picture is governed by the scrambling of initially simple operators into superpositions of exponentially many Pauli strings. The corresponding expansion coefficients define the Pauli spectrum, whose structure controls the performance of classical algorithms based on truncating Pauli expansions. Here we determine the finite-depth Pauli spectrum of random quantum circuits, both in the noiseless case and in the presence of local noise, through its moments, given by the operator stabilizer Rényi entropies. In noiseless circuits, we uncover a hierarchy in the approach to the fully scrambled regime: low moments equilibrate at relatively short depths, while higher moments, which are sensitive to rare, large-amplitude Pauli coefficients, require parametrically larger depths. In noisy circuits, scrambling competes with an effective suppression of operator spreading. Above a critical error per cycle $γ_c N=\mathcal{O}(1)$, the operator fails to reach the fully scrambled distribution and remains supported on an atypically sparse subset of Pauli strings. Conversely, below this scale, we rigorously show that classical simulation remains exponentially hard, demonstrating that finite noise does not automatically imply classical simulability. The resulting noise-induced transition in operator complexity therefore delineates the boundary between intrinsically hard quantum dynamics and those that remain classically accessible.


---


## 没有格子时布洛赫振荡的广义流体动力学

**Original Title:** Generalized Hydrodynamics of Bloch Oscillations in the Absence of a Lattice

**Authors:** Stefano Scopa, Philip Zechmann, Michael Knap, Jacopo De Nardis, Alvise Bastianello

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18957v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18957v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

受到恒定力的物体通常会随着时间的推移而增加速度。每当它们的能量是动量的平滑和周期性函数时，这种期望就会失败，从而导致周期性布洛赫振荡。周期性分散是格子系统的典型特征，也可以通过强相互作用在连续体媒体中出现。在这里，我们研究了可积分量子气体范式模型（双成分杨-高丁模型）中在没有格子的情况下这种布洛赫振荡现象。我们针对嵌入均匀相互作用背景中的有限密度的杂质推导出布洛赫振荡的广义流体动力学理论，我们表明由于质量中心的加速度，这种物质会持续叠加到漂移上。此外，我们还表明，当两磁振子束缚态被填充时，单杂质振荡周期在有限杂质密度下被重新正化。我们的结果与超冷原子实验相关，其中可以以可控的密度产生杂质。


### Abstract

Objects subjected to a constant force generally increase their velocity over time. This expectation fails whenever their energy is a smooth and periodic function of momentum, resulting in periodic Bloch oscillations instead. Periodic dispersions, typical of lattice systems, can also emerge in continuum media through strong interactions. Here, we study the phenomenon of such Bloch oscillations in the absence of a lattice in a paradigmatic model of integrable quantum gases: the two-component Yang-Gaudin model. We derive a generalized-hydrodynamic theory of Bloch oscillations for a finite density of impurities embedded in a homogeneous interacting background, which we show to persist superimposed to a drift due to the acceleration of the center of mass. Moreover, we show the single-impurity oscillation period is renormalized at finite impurity density when two-magnon bound states are populated. Our results are relevant for ultracold atom experiments, where impurities can be created at controllable densities.


---


## 2D导电量子位格子中W态的可扩展一步生成

**Original Title:** Scalable Single-Step Generation of W States in 2D Superconducting Qubit Lattices

**Authors:** João H. Romeiro, Federico A. Roy, Niklas Bruckmoser, Ivan Tsitsilin, Niklas J. Glaser, Christian M. F. Schneider, Gerhard B. P. Huber, Saya A. Schöbe, Johannes Schirk, Florian Wallner, Malay Singh, Julius Feigl, Leon Koch, Lasse Södergren, Max Werninghaus, Stefan Filipp

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18962v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18962v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

可靠地产生多量子位纠缠是大规模量子信息技术的先决条件。特别是，W州因其在当地损失或测量下的弹性而成为宝贵的资源。然而，用顺序的两量子位门准备这些状态通常需要大量的时间。相比之下，工程化的同时相互作用能够快速产生纠缠，即使在最近邻连接有限的量子位系统中也是如此。在这里，我们展示了一组快速且稳健的操作，用于在任意大小的网格上连贯地分布单个激发，从而直接从初始积状态生成W状态。在2D格子中，激发同时沿着两个方向传播，使得总纠缠时间仅随着最大维度而缩放。我们利用这一性质在99 ns内在3$x $2的超临界格子中制备了六量子位W状态，实现了83.9$$1.0%的断层摄影保真度。然后，我们扩展了该协议，以在最多7个量子位的链中创建纠缠，最大的W状态在264 ns内生成，保真度为79.6$\pm$1.3%。


### Abstract

The reliable generation of multi-qubit entanglement is a prerequisite for large-scale quantum information technologies. In particular, W states are a valuable resource owing to their resilience under local loss or measurement. Nevertheless, preparing these states with sequential two-qubit gates often requires substantial time overhead. By contrast, engineered simultaneous interactions enable fast entanglement generation, even in qubit systems with limited nearest-neighbour connectivity. Here, we demonstrate a set of fast and robust operations for coherently distributing a single excitation across a lattice of arbitrary size, thereby directly generating W states from initial product states. In 2D lattices, the excitation propagates along both directions simultaneously, such that the total entanglement time scales only with the largest dimension. We exploit this property to prepare a six-qubit W state in a 3$\times$2 superconducting lattice within 99 ns, achieving a tomographic fidelity of 83.9$\pm$1.0%. We then extend the protocol to create entanglement across chains of up to seven qubits, with the largest W state generated in 264 ns with a fidelity of 79.6$\pm$1.3%.


---


## 通过颜色布线的4D和5D层代码

**Original Title:** 4D and 5D Layer Codes through Color Routing

**Authors:** Andrew C. Yuan, Nouédyn Baspin

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18961v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18961v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们引入了显式的Calderbank-Shor-Steane（CSS）代码结构，将层代码推广到$D= 4，5 $维度。与其前身非常相似，本结构基于嵌入量子低密度检验（q低脂）码;从具有能垒$Δ$的$[[n，k，d]$码中，我们获得了具有参数$[[（n）]{D/（D-2）}），k，（dn）{1/（D-2）}]]$和能垒$««（A）$的$D= 4，5 $维层码。使用良好的q低脂码作为输入，我们的结构完全饱和了$D= 4，5 $维BPT界限。更高维度的层代码是模块化的，因此非常适合由模块化网络补丁组成的架构，尽管我们的物理限制在三维。我们通过使用\textit{Color Routing}克服了之前概括尝试中遇到的障碍，使我们能够解决检查层和线缺陷的结构。


### Abstract

We introduce and explicit Calderbank-Shor-Steane (CSS) code construction that generalizes the Layer codes to $D=4,5$ dimensions. Much like its predecessor, the present construction is based on embedding quantum low-density parity check (qLDPC) codes; from an $[[n,k,d]]$ code with energy barrier $Δ$, we obtain a $D=4,5$ dimensional Layer code with parameters $[[Θ(n^{D/(D-2)}), k, Θ(dn^{1/(D-2)})]]$ and energy barrier $Ω(Δ)$. Using good qLDPC codes as input, our construction saturates the $D=4,5$ dimensional BPT bounds exactly. The higher dimensional Layer Codes are modular, and thus well suited to architectures composed of modular network patches, despite our physical limitation to three dimensions. We overcome the hurdles encountered by previous generalization attempts through the use of \textit{color routing}, allowing us to resolve the structure of the check layers and line defects.

## 量子多体系统中的Clifford对称性

**Original Title:** Clifford symmetries in quantum many-body systems

**Authors:** Charlie Nation, Rick P. A. Simon, Shreya Banerjee, Francesco Martini, Alessandro Ricottone, Federico Cerisola, Luca Dellantonio

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18966v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18966v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

获得模型的对称性是理解并最终分析或数值求解模型的关键一步。然而，寻找对称性通常极其复杂，通常是有洞察力思考的结果。在这项工作中，我们用算法补充了人类的聪明才智。我们利用经典有效的Clifford群通过图表示来找到任意多体Hamilton体的对称性。我们在随机和物理Hamilton上展示了我们的方法，最多有一千个量子位的实例，并展示了我们的方法如何能够更深入地理解模型。


### Abstract

Obtaining the symmetries of a model is a critical step towards developing an understanding and ultimately analytically or numerically solving the model. However, finding symmetries is generally extremely complicated, often being the result of insightful thinking. In this work, we complement human ingenuity with an algorithm. We leverage the classically efficient Clifford group to find symmetries for arbitrary many-body Hamiltonians via a graph representation. We demonstrate our method on random and physical Hamiltonians, with instances of up to one thousand qubits and demonstrate how our approach can provide deeper understanding of the model.

## 非局部噪音磁力测量中高斯超涨落的特征

**Original Title:** Signatures of Gaussian superconducting fluctuations in nonlocal noise magnetometry

**Authors:** Dror Orgad

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18970v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18970v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们计算了由高斯超涨落引起的两点磁噪音谱，这是一个可以通过旋转量子位对（例如钻石中的氮空位中心）直接测量的量。该分析利用了与时间相关的金斯伯格-兰道理论，反映了波动库珀对当前相关性和随之而来的磁噪音的直接贡献。我们处理二维系统和电线，认为它们处于平衡状态和均匀电场下。预计高温超导体中的信号将最强，我们将我们的发现与涡旋液体的预测特征进行对比，以提供一种额外的途径来阐明这些系统中波动的性质。


### Abstract

We calculate the two-point magnetic noise spectrum arising from Gaussian superconducting fluctuations, a quantity directly measurable by spin qubit pairs such as nitrogen vacancy centers in diamond. The analysis utilizes the time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau theory, reflecting the direct contribution of fluctuating Cooper pairs to the current correlations and consequent magnetic noise. We treat both two-dimensional systems and wires, considering them in equilibrium and under a uniform electric field. The signal is expected to be strongest in high-temperature superconductors, and we contrast our findings with the predicted signatures of a vortex liquid to offer an additional route to elucidate the nature of fluctuations in these systems.

## 《伽罗瓦·库迪茨》评论

**Original Title:** A Review of Galois Qudits

**Authors:** Adam Wills

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18981v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18981v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

Galois quudits是$q$维量子系统，其泡利群的选择编码了某个有限域$\mathbb{F}_q$的算术。它们与更熟悉的模qudit不同，它们是相同的量子系统，但泡利群的选择是时钟和位移运算符，它们编码模$q$的整加法和乘的算术。Galois qudits是一种有用的数学结构，它使我们能够利用较大qudits固有的数学工具，同时只在物理上构建较小的qudits。特别是，维度$q = 2 ' s $的伽罗瓦量子比特与$s$量子比特的集合完全相同，不仅在其Hilbert空间中，而且在其泡利群和Clifford层次结构中。这种形式主义最近在在具有有用性质的量子位上构建量子误差纠正码方面发现了很大的用处。   在这篇评论中，我们在现有文献的基础上收集和形式化有关二元扩展域上的伽罗瓦quidits的事实和证明。我们定义了它们及其Clifford层次结构，描述了测量它们的泡利操作符的含义，描述了它们的稳定器表，正式定义了量子到量子位映射，最后描述了量子里德-所罗门码。


### Abstract

Galois qudits are $q$-dimensional quantum systems whose choice of Pauli group encodes the arithmetic of some finite field $\mathbb{F}_q$. They differ from the more familiar modular qudit, which are the same quantum system but whose choice of Pauli group are the clock and shift operators, which encode the arithmetic of integer addition and multiplication modulo $q$. Galois qudits are a useful mathematical construct that allow us to leverage the mathematical tools that are native to the larger qudit while only physically building smaller qudits. In particular, a Galois qudit of dimension $q = 2^s$ is exactly the same thing as a collection of $s$ qubits, not only in its Hilbert space, but also in its Pauli group, and Clifford hierarchy. This formalism has found a lot of utility recently in constructing quantum error-correcting codes over qubits with useful properties.
  In this review, we build on existing literature to collect and formalise facts and proofs about Galois qudits over binary extension fields. We define them and their Clifford hierarchies, describe what it means to measure their Pauli operators, describe their stabiliser tableaux, formally define qudit-to-qubit mappings, and finally describe quantum Reed-Solomon codes.


---


## 有效的基于傅里叶的正元线性组合及其在量子优化中的应用

**Original Title:** Efficient Fourier-Based Linear Combination of Unitaries and Applications in Quantum Optimization

**Authors:** Almudena Carrera Vazquez, Daniel J. Egger, Stefan Woerner

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18985v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18985v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们研究了无辅助线性么元组合（LCU）作为逼近复杂量子电路的框架。这对于量子优化算法尤其有效，其中候选解决方案可以进行经典评估，任务是对高质量位串进行采样，而不是再现完整的输出分布。我们表明，基于傅里叶的LCU构造可以有效地分解广泛的对角和非对角个位，用单量子位门层或明显更简单的结构取代高度连接的量子位相互作用，代价是付出了多项采样的代价。应用于QAOA等算法，这可以产生对基数约束惩罚和完全连接的XY混合器等高效、硬件友好的分解，同时与完全一致的实现相比保持严格的性能保证。此外，我们在基于傅里叶的量子罚分和拉格朗日松弛之间建立了正式的联系，为约束处理提供了统一的视角。我们使用12个量子位电路的精确状态载体模拟和106个超导量子位的大规模实验来验证我们的方法。我们的结果说明了通过LCU的近似采样如何系统地以电路复杂性换取采样费用，从而扩展了近期量子优化的实际范围。


### Abstract

We investigate ancilla-free linear combination of unitaries (LCU) as a framework for approximating complex quantum circuits. This is particularly effective for quantum optimization algorithms, where candidate solutions can be evaluated classically and the task is to sample high-quality bitstrings rather than reproduce the full output distribution. We show that Fourier-based LCU constructions efficiently decompose broad classes of diagonal and non-diagonal unitaries, replacing highly connected qubit interactions with single-qubit gate layers or significantly simpler structures at the cost of a polynomial sampling overhead. Applied to algorithms such as QAOA, this yields efficient, hardware-friendly decompositions of, for instance, cardinality-constraint penalties and the fully connected XY-mixer, while maintaining rigorous performance guarantees compared to fully coherent implementations. Furthermore, we establish a formal connection between Fourier-based quantum penalties and Lagrangian relaxation, offering a unified perspective on constraint handling. We validate our approach using exact statevector simulations of 12-qubit circuits and large-scale experiments on 106 superconducting qubits. Our results illustrate how approximate sampling via an LCU systematically trades circuit complexity for sampling overhead, extending the practical reach of near-term quantum optimization.


---


## 随机量子状态的非高斯性

**Original Title:** Non-Gaussianity of random quantum states

**Authors:** Filiberto Ares, Sara Murciano, Pasquale Calabrese

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18986v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.18986v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们研究典型量子状态中的费米子非高斯性，重点关注具有或不具有全局$U（1）$对称性的量子位的哈尔随机状态。使用Weingarten演算，我们推导出非高斯性的分析预测，非高斯性被定义为约化密度矩阵与其高斯化对应矩阵之间的相对熵。我们确定了两个由子系统和系统大小之间的比率$\ell/L$控制的状态。对于$\ell/L < 1/2$，非高斯性在缺乏对称性的情况下消失，因为典型的约化密度矩阵以指数方式接近最大混合状态。相反，在存在全局$U（1）$对称的情况下，它仍然很小但有限。相比之下，在$\ell/L > 1/2$制度中，非高斯性变得广泛。这些结果建立了随机状态下费米子非高斯性的典型标度，并分析了全局对称性的存在如何对其进行修改。


### Abstract

We study the fermionic non-Gaussianity in typical quantum states, focusing on Haar random states of qubits with or without a global $U(1)$ symmetry. Using the Weingarten calculus, we derive analytical predictions for the non-Gaussianity, defined as the relative entropy between the reduced density matrix and its Gaussianized counterpart. We identify two regimes controlled by the ratio between the subsystem and the system size, $\ell/L$. For $\ell/L < 1/2$, the non-Gaussianity vanishes in the absence of symmetries, because typical reduced density matrices are exponentially close to the maximally mixed state. In the presence of a global $U(1)$ symmetry, instead, it remains small but finite. By contrast, in the regime $\ell/L > 1/2$, the non-Gaussianity becomes extensive. These results establish the typical scaling of fermionic non-Gaussianity in random states and analyze how this is modified by the presence of global symmetries.


---


## 量子点链中的集体电荷测量：控制垒位占据和隧道电流

**Original Title:** Collective charge measurement in quantum dot chains: controlling barrier occupation and tunneling current

**Authors:** Alok Nath Singh, Rafael Sánchez, Andrew N. Jordan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19001v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.19001v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

我们研究了三量子点（TQD）系统中的非平衡输运，其中中心点充当离散隧道屏障，接受量子点接触（QPC）的连续监测，该接触与所有三个点电容性耦合，具有独立可调的强度。我们表明，这种全球测量方案以与单站点测量在定性上不同的方式影响交通。通过工程结构化去相，测量可以显着改善屏障占用和隧道电流。在强测量极限下，稳态变得独立于基本的Hamilton参数，并且对于合适的测量配置，阻挡占据率可以接近1/2。我们确定了一种最佳测量配置，可以最大限度地提高稳态电流，并表明通过简单的中心点读出方案可以实现接近最佳的性能。


### Abstract

We investigate nonequilibrium transport in a triple-quantum-dot (TQD) system, where the central dot acts as a discrete tunnel barrier, subject to continuous monitoring by a quantum point contact (QPC) that is capacitively coupled to all three dots with independently tunable strengths. We show that this global measurement scheme affects transport in a qualitatively distinct manner from single-site measurement. By engineering structured dephasing, measurement provides a significant improvement in the barrier occupation and tunneling current. In the strong-measurement limit, the steady state becomes independent of the underlying Hamiltonian parameters, and the barrier occupation can approach 1/2 for suitable measurement configurations. We identify an optimal measurement configuration that maximizes the steady-state current and show that near-optimal performance can be achieved with a simple central-dot readout scheme.

## 量子光谱的半经典平行轨道理论

**Original Title:** Semiclassical periodic-orbit theory for quantum spectra

**Authors:** Sebastian Müller, Martin Sieber

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19019v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.19019v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-18


### 摘要

古茨威勒的踪迹公式在量子混乱中占有核心地位，因为它通过将经典混乱系统中的量子能量级与经典周期轨道联系起来，为经典混乱系统中的量子能量级提供了半经典逼近。在这篇说教文章中，我们讨论了从费曼路径积分开始的轨迹公式的推导。然后，我们描述了如何使用踪迹公式来解释随机矩阵理论描述的量子能量级分布的普遍特征，并概述了相关工作。


### Abstract

Gutzwiller's trace formula has a central place in quantum chaos because it provides semiclassical approximations for quantum energy levels in classically chaotic systems by linking them to classical periodic orbits. In this didactic article, we discuss a derivation of the trace formula starting from the Feynman path integral. We then describe how the trace formula is used to explain universal features in the distribution of the quantum energy levels that are described by random matrix theory, and we give an overview of related work.
