## 量子和机器学习之间的软件--以及脉冲

**Original Title:** Software Between Quantum and Machine Learning -- And Down to Pulses

**Authors:** Maja Franz, Melvin Strobl, Jonathan Hunz, Lukas Scheller, Lucas van der Horst, Eileen Kuehn, Achim Streit, Wolfgang Mauerer

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21286v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.21286v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-20


### 摘要

当代量子计算平台本质上仍然是可编程物理系统，其控制通常是通过单一门抽象来调节的。虽然此类抽象提供了统一的接口，但它们掩盖了底层硬件的重要方面，并可能限制对其全部功能的利用。控制脉冲级别的直接操作提供了一种更具表达力和物理上忠实的范式，例如，可以实施量身定制的错误缓解和优化策略。然而，这种表达能力的提高是以量子软件开发复杂性更大为代价的，这就需要结构化且可访问的工具。   我们提出了一个软件框架，集成在QML-Essentials包中，扩展了量子机器学习（QML）方法，以涵盖脉冲级建模。通过在QML设置中嵌入量子最优控制技术，我们的方法能够实现基于门和脉冲级表示的无缝组合。该框架提供了一套全面的建模和分析能力。特别是，我们介绍了可组合的anomaly结构的基础上可互换的积木，并支持端到端的脉冲参数优化。受量子傅里叶模型核心作用的激励，我们进一步结合了一系列傅里叶分析诊断，并辅之以扩展的纠缠测量。所有性能关键组件都在使用JAX的高性能环境中实施，并由专用量子模拟器支持。总而言之，该框架促进了可重复和系统性的研究，同时弥合了抽象电路模型和硬件感知优化之间的概念和实践鸿沟。它为QML和量子控制交叉点的未来发展提供了坚实的基础。


### Abstract

Contemporary quantum computing platforms remain, in essence, programmable physical systems whose control is typically mediated through unitary gate abstractions. While such abstractions provide a uniform interface, they obscure important aspects of the underlying hardware and may limit the exploitation of its full capabilities. Direct operation at the control-pulse level offers a more expressive and physically faithful paradigm, enabling, for instance, the implementation of tailored error-mitigation and optimisation strategies. However, this increased expressivity comes at the cost of greater quantum software development complexity, necessitating structured and accessible tooling.
  We present a software framework, integrated within the QML-Essentials package, that extends quantum machine learning (QML) methodologies to encompass pulse-level modelling. By embedding quantum optimal control techniques within a QML setting, our approach enables the seamless combination of gate-based and pulse-level representations. The framework provides a comprehensive suite of modelling and analytical capabilities. In particular, we introduce composable ansatz constructions based on interchangeable building blocks, and support for end-to-end optimisation of pulse parameters. Motivated by the central role of quantum Fourier models, we further incorporate a range of Fourier-analytic diagnostics, complemented by extended measures of entanglement. All performance-critical components are implemented in a high-performance environment using JAX and supported by a dedicated quantum simulator. Taken together, the framework facilitates reproducible and systematic investigations, while bridging the conceptual and practical divide between abstract circuit models and hardware-aware optimisation. It provides a robust foundation for future developments at the intersection of QML and quantum control.


---


## 量子非局部性和设备独立随机性对有噪的信号通道具有鲁棒性

**Original Title:** Quantum Nonlocality and Device-Independent Randomness are Robust to Noisy Signaling Channels

**Authors:** Kuntal Sengupta, Lewis Wooltorton

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21293v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.21293v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-20


### 摘要

给定一对接受随机二进制输入并返回二进制输出的隔离设备，用户可以仅从观察到的数据中推断潜在机制是否可以经典地解释。贝尔定理进一步指出，如果设备对纠缠量子状态执行某些测量，则可以排除经典解释，从而支持与设备无关（DI）的加密协议的安全性。对于某些协议，例如在狭小空间中执行的协议，可能很难完美地执行贝尔定理中要求的非信号假设。这引发了一个问题：量子非定域性对此类缺陷是否稳健？我们表明，如果二进制通道在进行任何测量之前向另一方发送一方输入的有噪副本，则答案是肯定的。我们完全描述了这种情况下局部多胞体的顶点和刻面，并识别出证明非信号量子相关性的贝尔不等式。即使发送了近乎完美的输入副本，这也是可能的。我们继续表明，在这种情况下证明DI随机性时，所识别的不等式比Clauser-Horne-Shimony-Holt不等式对去极化噪音更稳健。此外，当双方都收到彼此输入的有噪副本并得出类似的结论时，我们描述了局部多胞形，从而留下了许多新的潜在贝尔不等式有待探索。


### Abstract

Given a pair of isolated devices that accept random binary inputs and return binary outputs, a user can deduce from the observed data alone if the underlying mechanism can be explained classically. Bell's theorem further states that a classical explanation can be ruled out if the devices perform certain measurements on an entangled quantum state, underpinning the security of cryptographic protocols that are device-independent (DI). For certain protocols, such as those performed in a tight space, it might be difficult to perfectly enforce the non-signaling assumption required in Bell's theorem. This prompts the question: is quantum nonlocality robust to such imperfections? We show that if a binary channel sends a noisy copy of one party's input to the other before any measurements take place, the answer is yes. We completely characterize the vertices and facets of the local polytope in this scenario, and identify Bell inequalities that certify non-signaling quantum correlations. This is possible even when a near perfect copy of the input is sent. We go on to show that the identified inequalities are more robust to depolarizing noise than the Clauser-Horne-Shimony-Holt inequality when certifying DI randomness in this scenario. In addition, we characterize the local polytope when both parties receive a noisy copy of each other's input and make similar conclusions, leaving many new potential Bell inequalities to be explored.


---


## 量子机器学习优势与数十个噪声量子比特的证据

**Original Title:** Evidence of Quantum Machine Learning Advantage with Tens of Noisy Qubits

**Authors:** Onur Danaci, Yash J. Patel, Riccardo Molteni, Evert van Nieuwenburg, Vedran Dunjko, Jan A. Krzywda

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21346v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.21346v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-20


### 摘要

涉及量子数据的学习问题是证明量子机器学习优势的自然候选者。最近的结果表明，对于某些任务和无噪音条件下，量子数据的一致处理优于固定测量方案，随后是经典处理。目前尚不确定这种性能差距是否会在有限规模下持续存在，并且存在当前量子设备不可避免的噪音。在这项工作中，我们对现有硬件在已知表现出渐进优势的学习问题上的性能进行了模拟和分析，现在受到有噪量子数据的影响。将相干量子处理直接与固定测量方案进行比较，我们的结果表明，在仅30到40个噪声量子比特的范围内，性能分离明显。在这种规模下，根本的瓶颈不再是经典计算，而是数据采集;将噪声相干协议与测量优先策略相匹配仍然需要数月甚至数年的测量。通过系统地评估硬件的限制，如状态准备，门错误，读出错误，连接性和相干时间，我们提供的证据表明，这样一个强大的学习优势的演示是可访问的短期设备。


### Abstract

Learning problems involving quantum data are natural candidates for demonstrating an advantage in quantum machine learning. Recent results indicate that, for certain tasks and under noiseless conditions, coherent processing of quantum data outperforms fixed-measurement schemes followed by classical processing. It remained uncertain whether this performance gap persists at a finite scale, and in the presence of noise that is unavoidable with current quantum devices. In this work, we present simulations and analysis of the performance of existing hardware on a learning problem known to exhibit asymptotic advantage, now subjected to noisy quantum data. Comparing coherent quantum processing directly against fixed-measurement schemes, our results demonstrate a clear performance separation at a scale of just 30 to 40 noisy qubits. Already at this scale, the fundamental bottleneck is no longer classical computation but data acquisition; matching the noisy coherent protocol with measure-first strategies would still require months or even years of measurements. By systematically evaluating hardware constraints such as state preparation, gate errors, readout errors, connectivity, and coherence times, we provide evidence that a demonstration of such a strong learning advantage is accessible on near-term devices.


---


## Jacobi运算的本质奇异极限及其在高级压缩中的应用

**Original Title:** Essentially singular limits of Jacobi operators and applications to higher-order squeezing

**Authors:** Felix Fischer, Daniel Burgarth, Davide Lonigro

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21355v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.21355v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-20


### 摘要

我们研究了一类Jacobi运算符，其中对角线项乘以耦合参数$X\geq 0 $。在适当的条件下，对于每一个$x>0$，该操作符都是自伴的，而$x =0$处的形式极限是一个对称Jacobi操作符，允许单参数族自伴扩张。我们分析的一个核心内容是推导小$范围下平方可和广义特征量的一致界，该范围将离散WKB方法与Airy函数渐进性相结合。使用这些估计，我们在强预解意义上分析了限制行为$| j | to 0 $，证明对于每个序列$| j | to 0 $，可以提取一个子序列，沿着该子序列相应的Jacobi运算符收敛到限制运算符的某个自伴随扩张;相反，每个这样的扩张都可以通过这种方式获得。通过类比复分析中的本质奇异性，我们将这种行为称为本质上的奇异极限。   作为应用，我们研究了量子光学中出现的高级压缩操作员。利用与Jacobi运算符的联系，我们表明，当自由场项的相对强度趋于零时，压缩运算符的不同自伴随扩张会沿着不同的序列选择。特别是，这个限制并没有挑选出物理上独特的自伴随扩展，而是识别出与基础对称性兼容的扩展的独特子集。


### Abstract

We study a family of Jacobi operators in which the diagonal entries are multiplied by a coupling parameter $λ\geq0$. Under suitable conditions, the operator is self-adjoint for every $λ>0$, while the formal limit at $λ=0$ is a symmetric Jacobi operator admitting a one-parameter family of self-adjoint extensions. A central ingredient of our analysis is the derivation of uniform bounds for square-summable generalized eigenvectors in the small-$λ$ regime, which combines discrete WKB methods with Airy-function asymptotics. Using these estimates, we analyze the limiting behavior $λ\to0$ in the strong resolvent sense, proving that for every sequence $λ_j\to0$ one can extract a subsequence along which the corresponding Jacobi operators converge to some self-adjoint extension of the limiting operator; conversely, every such extension can be obtained in this way. We call this behavior an essentially singular limit, by analogy with essential singularities in complex analysis.
  As an application, we study higher-order squeezing operators arising in quantum optics. Using the connection with Jacobi operators, we show that when the relative strength of the free-field term tends to zero, different self-adjoint extensions of the squeezing operator are selected along different sequences. In particular, this limit does not single out a physically distinguished self-adjoint extension, but instead identifies a distinguished subclass of extensions compatible with the underlying symmetry.


---


## 量子先知的建模与资源优化

**Original Title:** Modeling and Resource Optimization for Quantum Oracles

**Authors:** Zhihang Li, Bo Zhao, Chuanbing Han, Jie Zhao, Jinchen Xu, Guoqiang Shu, Yimin Gao, Woji He, Zheng Shan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21380v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.21380v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-20


### 摘要

量子计算在特定应用中展示了其相对于超级计算的显着优势，并显示出广阔的前景，例如机器学习、密码学、金融等。量子Oracle在许多量子算法中非常常见，Oracle资源消耗直接影响算法性能。然而，现有的Oracle设计通常表现出高的资源负担和有限的兼容性。此外，缺乏结构化描述工具和复杂性分析方法。在这项工作中，我们引入了分层回归合成评估（HRSE）模型，实现了对先知的形式化描述和精确的量子门复杂性分析。基于这个模型，我们提出了一种自适应空间深度权衡（ASDT）算法，用于在固定量子位约束下生成Oracle结构。我们提供了一个理论证明，表明ASDT算法对于给定数量的量子位实现了最佳门计数。实验结果表明，与W循环方法相比，ASDT算法将平均量子电路深度减少了53.99%，变量数分别为10、15和20。


### Abstract

Quantum computing has demonstrated its significant advantage over supercomputing for specific applications and shown promising prospect, such as machine learning, cryptography, finance, etc.. Quantum oracles are very common in many quantum algorithms and oracle resource consumption directly affects algorithm performance. However, existing oracle designs often exhibit high resource overhead and limited compatibility. Moreover, structured description tools and complexity analysis methods are lacked. In this work, we introduces a Hierarchical Recursive Synthesis-Evaluation (HRSE) model, enabling formal description and precise quantum gate complexity analysis of oracles. Based on this model, we propose an Adaptive Space-depth Trade-off (ASDT) algorithm for generating oracle structures under a fixed qubit constraint. We provide a theoretical proof showing that the ASDT algorithm achieves the optimal gate count for a given number of qubits. Experimental results show that the ASDT algorithm reduces the average quantum circuit depth by 53.99% compared with the W-cycle approach, with the number of variables being 10, 15, and 20, respectively.


---


## 将非参数量子状态和MERA张量网络结合起来进行接地状态优化

**Original Title:** Combining non-parametric quantum states and MERA tensor networks for ground-state optimization

**Authors:** Julian Schuhmacher, Alberto Baiardi, Francesco Tacchino, Ivano Tavernelli

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21447v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.21447v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-20


### 摘要

混合张量网络提供了一条有希望的途径，可以通过合并在量子计算机上准备的量子状态来增强经典张量网络方法的表达能力。现有的方法受到张量网络量子分量的变分优化的限制。在这项工作中，我们引入了一种替代策略，该策略结合了通过量子模拟制备的非参数量子状态和经典的等距张量网络。后者经过变分优化，而前者则用作经典阴影形式的固定边界张量资源。我们通过对横向场伊辛模型的广泛数值模拟证明了这种方法的可行性，表明优化过程在统计和硬件噪音下仍然保持稳健。此外，我们的结果表明，与原始量子模拟相比，我们新提出的设置提高了所获得的底薪逼近的准确性，而不会增加应用量子电路的深度。因此，这种设置提供了一条将变分量子算法扩展到量子效用规模的实用途径。


### Abstract

Hybrid tensor networks offer a promising route to enhance the expressivity of classical tensor network methods by incorporating quantum states prepared on a quantum computer. Existing approaches are limited by the variational optimization of the quantum component of the tensor network. In this work, we introduce an alternative strategy that combines a non-parametric quantum state prepared through quantum annealing and a classical isometric tensor network. The latter is variationally optimized while the former is used as a fixed, boundary tensor resource in the form of classical shadows. We demonstrate the feasibility of this approach through extensive numerical simulations on the transverse-field Ising model, showing that the optimization procedure remains robust under statistical and hardware noise. Moreover, our results indicate that our newly proposed setup improves the accuracy of the obtained ground state approximation compared to the original quantum simulation, without increasing the depth of the applied quantum circuits. Therefore, this setup offers a practical route to scale variational quantum algorithms towards the quantum utility scale.


---


## 相干量子推理的指数样本复杂性优势

**Original Title:** An Exponential Sample-Complexity Advantage for Coherent Quantum Inference

**Authors:** Zhaoyi Li, Elias Theil, Aram W. Harrow, Isaac Chuang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21457v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2605.21457v1

**Submitted:** 2026-05-20


### 摘要

标准量子推理将量子数据转换为经典输出。我们研究了一种替代推理设置，其中所需的输出是量子的，并保持了一致性。此类设置包括量子纯度放大（QPA）、混合状态近似纯化或克隆以及密度矩阵取指数。我们表明，此类协议可以实现比不连贯的、测量介导的协议呈指数级低的样本复杂性。对于具有主本征状态目标和$d$维输入的QPA，一致处理使用$O（1/\varepð）$副本来实现错误$\varepð $，而不是任何不一致协议所需的$（d/\varepð）$副本。这些尖锐的连贯-非连贯分离共同催生了连贯量子推理理论，其中纠缠破坏极限识别了每个连贯协议的最佳非连贯对应物。


### Abstract

Standard quantum inference converts quantum data into classical outputs. We study an alternative inference setting in which the desired output is quantum, preserving coherence. Such settings include quantum purity amplification (QPA), mixed-state approximate purification or cloning, and density matrix exponentiation. We show that such protocols can achieve exponentially lower sample complexity than incoherent, measurement-mediated protocols. For QPA with principal eigenstate targets and $d$-dimensional inputs, coherent processing achieves error $\varepsilon$ using $O(1/\varepsilon)$ copies, versus the $Ω(d/\varepsilon)$ copies required by any incoherent protocol. Together, these sharp coherent-incoherent separations seed a theory of coherent quantum inference, with an entanglement-breaking limit identifying the optimal incoherent counterpart of each coherent protocol.


---
